id='LC2'><br/></div><div class='line' id='LC3'>Version: 8.0</div><div class='line' id='LC4'>Author : Shougo &lt;Shougo.Matsu@gmail.com&gt;</div><div class='line' id='LC5'>License: MIT license class='line' id='LC9'>&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;without limitation the rights to use, copy, modify, merge, publish,</div><div class='line' id='LC10'>&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;distribute, sublicense, and/or sell copies of the Software, and to</div><div class='line' id='LC11'>&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;permit persons to whom the Software is furnished to do so, subject to</div><div class='line' id='LC12'>&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;the following conditions:</div><div class='line' id='LC13'>&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;The above copyright notice and this permission notice shall be included</div><div class='line' id='LC14'>&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;in all copies or substantial portions of the Software.</div><div class='line' id='LC15'><br/></div><div class='line' id='LC16'>&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;THE SOFTWARE IS PROVIDED &quot;AS IS&quot;, WITHOUT WARRANTY OF ANY KIND, EXPRESS</div><div class='line' id='LC17'>&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;OR IMPLIED, INCLUDING BUT NOT LIMITED TO THE WARRANTIES OF</div><div class='line' id='LC18'>&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;MERCHANTABILITY, FITNESS FOR A PARTICULAR PURPOSE AND NONINFRINGEMENT.</div><div class='line' id='LC19'>&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;IN NO EVENT SHALL THE AUTHORS OR COPYRIGHT HOLDERS BE LIABLE FOR ANY</div><div class='line' id='LC20'>&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;CLAIM, DAMAGES OR OTHER LIABILITY, WHETHER IN AN ACTION OF CONTRACT,</div><div class='line' id='LC21'>&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;TORT OR OTHERWISE, ARISING FROM, OUT OF OR IN CONNECTION WITH THE</div><div class='line' id='LC22'>&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;SOFTWARE OR THE USE OR OTHER DEALINGS IN THE SOFTWARE.</div><div class='line' id='LC23'>}}}</div><div class='line' id='LC24'><br/></div><div class='line' id='LC25'>CONTENTS					*neocomplcache-contents*</div><div class='line' id='LC26'><br/></div><div class='line' id='LC27'>Introduction		|neocomplcache-introduction|</div><div class='line' id='LC28'>Install			|neocomplcache-install|</div><div class='line' id='LC29'>Interface		|neocomplcache-interface|</div><div class='line' id='LC30'>&nbsp;&nbsp;Commands		  |neocomplcache-commands|</div><div class='line' id='LC31'>&nbsp;&nbsp;Variables		  |neocomplcache-variables|</div><div class='line' id='LC32'>&nbsp;&nbsp;Key mappings		  |neocomplcache-key-mappings|</div><div class='line' id='LC33'>&nbsp;&nbsp;Functions		  |neocomplcache-functions|</div><div class='line' id='LC34'>Examples		|neocomplcache-examples|</div><div class='line' id='LC35'>Sources			|neocomplcache-sources|</div><div class='line' id='LC36'>&nbsp;&nbsp;User sources		  |neocomplcache-user-sources|</div><div class='line' id='LC37'>Create source		|neocomplcache-create-source|</div><div class='line' id='LC38'>&nbsp;&nbsp;Source attributes       |neocomplcache-source-attributes|</div><div class='line' id='LC39'>&nbsp;&nbsp;Candidate attributes   |neocomplcache-candidate-attributes|</div><div class='line' id='LC40'>Create filter		|neocomplcache-create-filter|</div><div class='line' id='LC41'>&nbsp;&nbsp;Filter attributes       |neocomplcache-filter-attributes|</div><div class='line' id='LC42'>FILTERS			|neocomplcache-filters|</div><div class='line' id='LC43'>FAQ			|neocomplcache-faq|</div><div class='line' id='LC44'><br/></div><div class='line' id='LC45'>==============================================================================</div><div class='line' id='LC46'>INTRODUCTION					*neocomplcache-introduction*</div><div class='line' id='LC47'><br/></div><div class='line' id='LC48'>*neocomplcache* is the abbreviation of &quot;neo-completion with cache&quot;. It</div><div class='line' id='LC49'>provides keyword completion system by maintaining a cache of keywords in the</div><div class='line' id='LC50'>current buffer. neocomplcache could be customized easily and has a lot more</div><div class='line' id='LC51'>features than the Vim&#39;s standard completion feature.</div><div class='line' id='LC52'>Note: neocomplcache may consume more memory than other plugins.</div><div class='line' id='LC53'><br/></div><div class='line' id='LC54'>Note: If you use Vim 7.3.885 or above with if\_lua feature, you should use</div><div class='line' id='LC55'>neocomplete.  It is faster than neocomplcache.</div><div class='line' id='LC56'><br/></div><div class='line' id='LC57'>https://github.com/Shougo/neocomplete.vim</div><div class='line' id='LC58'><br/></div><div class='line' id='LC59'>==============================================================================</div><div class='line' id='LC60'>INSTALL						*neocomplcache-install*</div><div class='line' id='LC61'><br/></div><div class='line' id='LC62'>1: Extract the file and put files in your Vim directory</div><div class='line' id='LC63'>&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;(usually ~/.vim/ or Program Files/Vim/vimfiles on Windows).</div><div class='line' id='LC64'>2: Execute |:NeoComplCacheEnable| command or set</div><div class='line' id='LC65'>let g:neocomplcache_enable_at_startup = 1</div><div class='line' id='LC66'>in your .vimrc.</div><div class='line' id='LC67'><br/></div><div class='line' id='LC68'>						*neocomplcache-asynchronous*</div><div class='line' id='LC69'>*neocomplcache-RECOMMENDATION*</div><div class='line' id='LC70'>With neocomplcache Ver.6.0 or later, when you have |vimproc| installed,</div><div class='line' id='LC71'>neocomplcache creates caches asynchronously.</div><div class='line' id='LC72'><br/></div><div class='line' id='LC73'>vimproc is distributed at: http://github.com/Shougo/vimproc</div><div class='line' id='LC74'><br/></div><div class='line' id='LC75'>To use vimproc, you must compile it.  Refer to the vimproc documentation.</div><div class='line' id='LC76'><br/></div><div class='line' id='LC77'>Note: Snippets feature (snippets_complete source), which was originally</div><div class='line' id='LC78'>&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;built-in, left since neocomplcache ver.7.</div><div class='line' id='LC79'>&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;If you were using it, please install neosnippet source manually.</div><div class='line' id='LC80'><br/></div><div class='line' id='LC81'>https://github.com/Shougo/neosnippet</div><div class='line' id='LC82'><br/></div><div class='line' id='LC83'>==============================================================================</div><div class='line' id='LC84'>INTERFACE					*neocomplcache-interface*</div><div class='line' id='LC85'><br/></div><div class='line' id='LC86'>------------------------------------------------------------------------------</div><div class='line' id='LC87'>COMMANDS 					*neocomplcache-commands*</div><div class='line' id='LC88'><br/></div><div class='line' id='LC89'>:NeoComplCacheEnable				*:NeoComplCacheEnable*</div><div class='line' id='LC90'>		Validate neocomplcache and initialize it.</div><div class='line' id='LC91'>		Warning: Conventional cache disappears.</div><div class='line' id='LC92'><br/></div><div class='line' id='LC93'>:NeoComplCacheDisable				*:NeoComplCacheDisable*</div><div class='line' id='LC94'>		Invalidate neocomplcache and clean it up.</div><div class='line' id='LC95'><br/></div><div class='line' id='LC96'>:NeoComplCacheToggle				*:NeoComplCacheToggle*</div><div class='line' id='LC97'>		Change a lock state of neocomplcache.</div><div class='line' id='LC98'>		While neocomplcache is in locking, you cannot use automatic</div><div class='line' id='LC99'>		completions.</div><div class='line' id='LC100'>		Note: This command enables neocomplcache when neocomplcache is</div><div class='line' id='LC101'>		already disabled.</div><div class='line' id='LC102'><br/></div><div class='line' id='LC103'>:Neco [{anim-number}] 				*:Neco*</div><div class='line' id='LC104'>		Secret.</div><div class='line' id='LC105'><br/></div><div class='line' id='LC106'>:NeoComplCacheLock				*:NeoComplCacheLock*</div><div class='line' id='LC107'>		Lock neocomplcache.</div><div class='line' id='LC108'>		While neocomplcache is in locking, you cannot use automatic</div><div class='line' id='LC109'>		completions but can use manual completions.</div><div class='line' id='LC110'>		The lock status is local to each buffer.</div><div class='line' id='LC111'>		Note: This command is disabled when neocomplcache is disabled.</div><div class='line' id='LC112'><br/></div><div class='line' id='LC113'>:NeoComplCacheUnlock				*:NeoComplCacheUnlock*</div><div class='line' id='LC114'>		Unlock neocomplcache.</div><div class='line' id='LC115'>		Note: This command is disabled when neocomplcache is disabled.</div><div class='line' id='LC116'><br/></div><div class='line' id='LC117'>:NeoComplCacheLockSource {source-name}		*:NeoComplCacheLockSource*</div><div class='line' id='LC118'>		Disable {source-name} source completion.  Disable state is</div><div class='line' id='LC119'>		local to each buffer.</div><div class='line' id='LC120'><br/></div><div class='line' id='LC121'>:NeoComplCacheUnlockSource {source-name}	*:NeoComplCacheUnlockSource*</div><div class='line' id='LC122'>		Unlock {source-name} source completion.</div><div class='line' id='LC123'><br/></div><div class='line' id='LC124'>					*:NeoComplCacheAutoCompletionLength*</div><div class='line' id='LC125'>:NeoComplCacheAutoCompletionLength {length}</div><div class='line' id='LC126'>		Change start length of automatic completion to {length}.</div><div class='line' id='LC127'>		Note: This length value is local to each buffer.</div><div class='line' id='LC128'><br/></div><div class='line' id='LC129'>:NeoComplCacheCachingBuffer [bufname]		*:NeoComplCacheCachingBuffer*</div><div class='line' id='LC130'>		Cache [bufname] buffer.</div><div class='line' id='LC131'>		Warning: it may take time considerably for the big buffer.</div><div class='line' id='LC132'>		This selects current buffer when you omitted [bufname].  When</div><div class='line' id='LC133'>		[bufname] buffer is not cached, this performs only simple</div><div class='line' id='LC134'>		caching.  If [bufname] is not loaded, neocomplcache will open</div><div class='line' id='LC135'>		[bufname] automatically.</div><div class='line' id='LC136'><br/></div><div class='line' id='LC137'>:NeoComplCacheCachingSyntax [filetype]		*:NeoComplCacheCachingSyntax*</div><div class='line' id='LC138'>		Caches [filetype] syntax file.</div><div class='line' id='LC139'>		Selects current buffer filetype when [filetype] is omitted.</div><div class='line' id='LC140'><br/></div><div class='line' id='LC141'>:NeoComplCacheCachingDictionary [filetype]</div><div class='line' id='LC142'>					*:NeoComplCacheCachingDictionary*</div><div class='line' id='LC143'>		Caches [filetype] dictionary file.</div><div class='line' id='LC144'>		Selects current buffer filetype when [filetype] is omitted.</div><div class='line' id='LC145'><br/></div><div class='line' id='LC146'>:NeoComplCacheCachingTags		*:NeoComplCacheCachingTags*</div><div class='line' id='LC147'>		Caches tags file in current buffer.</div><div class='line' id='LC148'><br/></div><div class='line' id='LC149'>:NeoComplCacheCachingInclude [bufname]		*:NeoComplCacheCachingInclude*</div><div class='line' id='LC150'>		Caches [bufname] include file.</div><div class='line' id='LC151'>		Selects current buffer name when [bufname] is omitted.</div><div class='line' id='LC152'><br/></div><div class='line' id='LC153'>:NeoComplCachePrintSource [bufname]		*:NeoComplCachePrintSource*</div><div class='line' id='LC154'>		Outputs [bufname] buffer&#39;s cache in current buffer.</div><div class='line' id='LC155'>		This command is for debugging.</div><div class='line' id='LC156'>		Selects current buffer when [bufname] is omitted.</div><div class='line' id='LC157'>		For a command for debugging, a user will not need to use it</div><div class='line' id='LC158'>		mainly.</div><div class='line' id='LC159'><br/></div><div class='line' id='LC160'>:NeoComplCacheOutputKeyword [bufname]		*:NeoComplCacheOutputKeyword*</div><div class='line' id='LC161'>		Write the keyword which cached [bufname] buffer in current</div><div class='line' id='LC162'>		buffer.  Select current buffer when [bufname] omitted.  When</div><div class='line' id='LC163'>		you make a dictionary file by yourself, it may be</div><div class='line' id='LC164'>		convenient.</div><div class='line' id='LC165'><br/></div><div class='line' id='LC166'><br/></div><div class='line' id='LC167'>:NeoComplCacheSetFileType [filetype]		*:NeoComplCacheSetFileType*</div><div class='line' id='LC168'>		Change filetype to [filetype] in current buffer.</div><div class='line' id='LC169'>		This filetype is only used neocomplcache.</div><div class='line' id='LC170'>		Note: You can get current filetype by</div><div class='line' id='LC171'>		|neocomplcache#get_context_filetype()|</div><div class='line' id='LC172'><br/></div><div class='line' id='LC173'>:NeoComplCacheClean 				*:NeoComplCacheClean*</div><div class='line' id='LC174'>		Clean cache files in |g:neocomplcache_temporary_dir|.</div><div class='line' id='LC175'><br/></div><div class='line' id='LC176'>------------------------------------------------------------------------------</div><div class='line' id='LC177'>VARIABLES 					*neocomplcache-variables*</div><div class='line' id='LC178'><br/></div><div class='line' id='LC179'>					*g:neocomplcache_enable_at_startup*</div><div class='line' id='LC180'>g:neocomplcache_enable_at_startup</div><div class='line' id='LC181'>		Neocomplcache gets started automatically when Vim starts if</div><div class='line' id='LC182'>		this value is 1.</div><div class='line' id='LC183'><br/></div><div class='line' id='LC184'>		With the default value 0, you cannot use neocomplcache</div><div class='line' id='LC185'>		unless you start it manually.</div><div class='line' id='LC186'><br/></div><div class='line' id='LC187'>		Note: This option has to be set in .vimrc or _vimrc.  NOT IN</div><div class='line' id='LC188'>		.gvimrc nor _gvimrc!</div><div class='line' id='LC189'><br/></div><div class='line' id='LC190'>g:neocomplcache_max_list			*g:neocomplcache_max_list*</div><div class='line' id='LC191'>		This variable controls the number of candidates displayed in a</div><div class='line' id='LC192'>		pop-up menu.  Candidates more than this value won&#39;t be show</div><div class='line' id='LC193'>		up.</div><div class='line' id='LC194'><br/></div><div class='line' id='LC195'>		Default value is 100.</div><div class='line' id='LC196'><br/></div><div class='line' id='LC197'>					*g:neocomplcache_max_keyword_width*</div><div class='line' id='LC198'>g:neocomplcache_max_keyword_width</div><div class='line' id='LC199'>		This variable controls the indication width of a candidate</div><div class='line' id='LC200'>		displayed in a pop-up menu.  The case beyond this value is</div><div class='line' id='LC201'>		cut down properly.</div><div class='line' id='LC202'><br/></div><div class='line' id='LC203'>		Default value is 80.</div><div class='line' id='LC204'><br/></div><div class='line' id='LC205'>					*g:neocomplcache_max_menu_width*</div><div class='line' id='LC206'>g:neocomplcache_max_menu_width</div><div class='line' id='LC207'>		This variable controls the indication width of a menu</div><div class='line' id='LC208'>		displayed in a pop-up menu.  The case beyond this value is cut</div><div class='line' id='LC209'>		down.</div><div class='line' id='LC210'><br/></div><div class='line' id='LC211'>		Default value is 15.</div><div class='line' id='LC212'><br/></div><div class='line' id='LC213'>				*g:neocomplcache_auto_completion_start_length*</div><div class='line' id='LC214'>g:neocomplcache_auto_completion_start_length</div><div class='line' id='LC215'>		This variable controls the number of the input completion</div><div class='line' id='LC216'>		at the time of key input automatically.</div><div class='line' id='LC217'>		Note: |g:neocomplcache_auto_completion_start_length| is used</div><div class='line' id='LC218'>		for &quot;keyword&quot; kind source only. Please refer to</div><div class='line' id='LC219'>			|neocomplcache-source-attribute-min_pattern_length|.</div><div class='line' id='LC220'><br/></div><div class='line' id='LC221'>		Default value is 2.</div><div class='line' id='LC222'><br/></div><div class='line' id='LC223'>			*g:neocomplcache_manual_completion_start_length*</div><div class='line' id='LC224'>g:neocomplcache_manual_completion_start_length</div><div class='line' id='LC225'>		This variable controls the number of the input completion</div><div class='line' id='LC226'>		at the time of manual completion.  It is convenient when you</div><div class='line' id='LC227'>		reduce this value, but may get heavy when you deleted a</div><div class='line' id='LC228'>		letter in &lt;C-h&gt; or &lt;BS&gt; at popup indication time.</div><div class='line' id='LC229'><br/></div><div class='line' id='LC230'>		Default value is 0.</div><div class='line' id='LC231'><br/></div><div class='line' id='LC232'>					*g:neocomplcache_min_keyword_length*</div><div class='line' id='LC233'>g:neocomplcache_min_keyword_length</div><div class='line' id='LC234'>		In a buffer or dictionary files, this variable controls</div><div class='line' id='LC235'>		length of keyword becoming the object of the completion at</div><div class='line' id='LC236'>		the minimum.</div><div class='line' id='LC237'><br/></div><div class='line' id='LC238'>		Default value is 4.</div><div class='line' id='LC239'><br/></div><div class='line' id='LC240'>					*g:neocomplcache_min_syntax_length*</div><div class='line' id='LC241'>g:neocomplcache_min_syntax_length</div><div class='line' id='LC242'>		In syntax files, this variable controls length of keyword</div><div class='line' id='LC243'>		becoming the object of the completion at the minimum.</div><div class='line' id='LC244'><br/></div><div class='line' id='LC245'>		Default value is 4.</div><div class='line' id='LC246'><br/></div><div class='line' id='LC247'>					*g:neocomplcache_enable_ignore_case*</div><div class='line' id='LC248'>g:neocomplcache_enable_ignore_case</div><div class='line' id='LC249'>		When neocomplcache looks for candidate completion, this</div><div class='line' id='LC250'>		variable controls whether neocomplcache ignores the upper-</div><div class='line' id='LC251'>		and lowercase.  If it is 1, neocomplcache ignores case.</div><div class='line' id='LC252'><br/></div><div class='line' id='LC253'>		Default value is &#39;ignorecase&#39;.</div><div class='line' id='LC254'><br/></div><div class='line' id='LC255'>					*g:neocomplcache_enable_smart_case*</div><div class='line' id='LC256'>g:neocomplcache_enable_smart_case</div><div class='line' id='LC257'>		When a capital letter is included in input, neocomplcache does</div><div class='line' id='LC258'>		not ignore the upper- and lowercase.</div><div class='line' id='LC259'><br/></div><div class='line' id='LC260'>		Default value is &#39;infercase&#39;.</div><div class='line' id='LC261'><br/></div><div class='line' id='LC262'>				*g:neocomplcache_disable_auto_complete*</div><div class='line' id='LC263'>g:neocomplcache_disable_auto_complete</div><div class='line' id='LC264'>		This variable controls whether you invalidate automatic</div><div class='line' id='LC265'>		completion.  If it is 1, automatic completion becomes</div><div class='line' id='LC266'>		invalid, but can use the manual completion by &lt;C-x&gt;&lt;C-u&gt;.</div><div class='line' id='LC267'><br/></div><div class='line' id='LC268'>		Default value is 0.</div><div class='line' id='LC269'><br/></div><div class='line' id='LC270'>					*g:neocomplcache_enable_wildcard*</div><div class='line' id='LC271'>g:neocomplcache_enable_wildcard</div><div class='line' id='LC272'>		This variable controls whether neocomplcache accept wild</div><div class='line' id='LC273'>		card character &#39;*&#39; for input-saving.</div><div class='line' id='LC274'>		Note: You can customize the wildcard character by</div><div class='line' id='LC275'>		|g:neocomplcache_wildcard_characters|.</div><div class='line' id='LC276'><br/></div><div class='line' id='LC277'>		Default value is 1.</div><div class='line' id='LC278'><br/></div><div class='line' id='LC279'>					*g:neocomplcache_enable_cursor_hold_i*</div><div class='line' id='LC280'>g:neocomplcache_enable_cursor_hold_i</div><div class='line' id='LC281'>		This variable controls whether neocomplcache use |CursorHoldI|</div><div class='line' id='LC282'>		event when complete candidates.</div><div class='line' id='LC283'>		Note: You should not use this option if less than Vim 7.3.418.</div><div class='line' id='LC284'>		Note: This option must be set before call</div><div class='line' id='LC285'>		|:NeoComplCacheEnable|.</div><div class='line' id='LC286'><br/></div><div class='line' id='LC287'>		Default value is 0.</div><div class='line' id='LC288'><br/></div><div class='line' id='LC289'>					*g:neocomplcache_cursor_hold_i_time*</div><div class='line' id='LC290'>g:neocomplcache_cursor_hold_i_time</div><div class='line' id='LC291'>		If g:neocomplcache_enable_cursor_hold_i is non-zero and in</div><div class='line' id='LC292'>		insert mode, this value changes &#39;updatetime&#39; option.</div><div class='line' id='LC293'><br/></div><div class='line' id='LC294'>		Default value is 300.</div><div class='line' id='LC295'><br/></div><div class='line' id='LC296'>				*g:neocomplcache_enable_insert_char_pre*</div><div class='line' id='LC297'>g:neocomplcache_enable_insert_char_pre</div><div class='line' id='LC298'>		This variable controls whether neocomplcache use</div><div class='line' id='LC299'>		|InsertCharPre| event when complete candidates.</div><div class='line' id='LC300'>		Note: You should not use this option if less than Vim 7.3.461.</div><div class='line' id='LC301'>		Note: This option must be set before call</div><div class='line' id='LC302'>		|:NeoComplCacheEnable|.</div><div class='line' id='LC303'>		Note: This option is experimental.</div><div class='line' id='LC304'><br/></div><div class='line' id='LC305'>		Default value is 0.</div><div class='line' id='LC306'><br/></div><div class='line' id='LC307'>					*g:neocomplcache_enable_auto_select*</div><div class='line' id='LC308'>g:neocomplcache_enable_auto_select</div><div class='line' id='LC309'>		When neocomplcache displays candidates, this option controls</div><div class='line' id='LC310'>		whether neocomplcache selects the first candidate</div><div class='line' id='LC311'>		automatically.  If you enable this option, neocomplcache&#39;s</div><div class='line' id='LC312'>		completion behavior is like |AutoComplPop|.</div><div class='line' id='LC313'><br/></div><div class='line' id='LC314'>		Default value is 0.</div><div class='line' id='LC315'><br/></div><div class='line' id='LC316'>				*g:neocomplcache_enable_auto_delimiter*</div><div class='line' id='LC317'>g:neocomplcache_enable_auto_delimiter</div><div class='line' id='LC318'>		This option controls whether neocomplcache insert delimiter</div><div class='line' id='LC319'>		automatically.  For example, /(filename) or #(Vim script).</div><div class='line' id='LC320'><br/></div><div class='line' id='LC321'>		Default value is 0.</div><div class='line' id='LC322'><br/></div><div class='line' id='LC323'>				*g:neocomplcache_enable_camel_case_completion*</div><div class='line' id='LC324'>g:neocomplcache_enable_camel_case_completion</div><div class='line' id='LC325'>		When you input a capital letter, this variable controls</div><div class='line' id='LC326'>		whether neocomplcache takes an ambiguous searching as an end</div><div class='line' id='LC327'>		of the words in it.  For example, neocomplcache comes to match</div><div class='line' id='LC328'>		it with &quot;ArgumentsException&quot; when you input it with &quot;AE&quot;.</div><div class='line' id='LC329'><br/></div><div class='line' id='LC330'>		Note: This feature may be too slow.</div><div class='line' id='LC331'><br/></div><div class='line' id='LC332'>		Default value is 0.</div><div class='line' id='LC333'><br/></div><div class='line' id='LC334'>				*g:neocomplcache_enable_underbar_completion*</div><div class='line' id='LC335'>g:neocomplcache_enable_underbar_completion</div><div class='line' id='LC336'>		When you input _, this variable controls whether</div><div class='line' id='LC337'>		neocomplcache takes an ambiguous searching as an end of the</div><div class='line' id='LC338'>		words in it.  For example, neocomplcache comes to match it</div><div class='line' id='LC339'>		with &quot;public_html&quot; when you input it with &quot;p_h&quot;.</div><div class='line' id='LC340'><br/></div><div class='line' id='LC341'>		Note: This feature may be too slow.</div><div class='line' id='LC342'><br/></div><div class='line' id='LC343'>		Default value is 0.</div><div class='line' id='LC344'><br/></div><div class='line' id='LC345'>				*g:neocomplcache_enable_fuzzy_completion*</div><div class='line' id='LC346'>g:neocomplcache_enable_fuzzy_completion</div><div class='line' id='LC347'>		When you input one character, this variable controls whether</div><div class='line' id='LC348'>		neocomplcache takes an ambiguous searching as an end of the</div><div class='line' id='LC349'>		words in it.  For example, neocomplcache comes to match it with</div><div class='line' id='LC350'>		&quot;public_html&quot; or &quot;PublicHtml&quot; when you input it with &quot;puh&quot;.</div><div class='line' id='LC351'><br/></div><div class='line' id='LC352'>		Note: If you enable it,</div><div class='line' id='LC353'>		|g:neocomplcache_enable_underbar_completion| and</div><div class='line' id='LC354'>		|g:neocomplcache_enable_camel_case_completion| is disabled.</div><div class='line' id='LC355'><br/></div><div class='line' id='LC356'>		Note: If |g:neocomplcache_fuzzy_completion_start_length| is 3,</div><div class='line' id='LC357'>		&quot;ph&quot; does not complete &quot;public_html&quot;.</div><div class='line' id='LC358'><br/></div><div class='line' id='LC359'>		Note: This match is too heavy.  So, it is enabled when your</div><div class='line' id='LC360'>		input length is longer than or equal to</div><div class='line' id='LC361'>		|g:neocomplcache_fuzzy_completion_start_length| and less than</div><div class='line' id='LC362'>		20 characters.</div><div class='line' id='LC363'><br/></div><div class='line' id='LC364'>		Default value is 0.</div><div class='line' id='LC365'><br/></div><div class='line' id='LC366'>			*g:neocomplcache_fuzzy_completion_start_length*</div><div class='line' id='LC367'>g:neocomplcache_fuzzy_completion_start_length</div><div class='line' id='LC368'>		It controls length of fuzzy completion start length.  For</div><div class='line' id='LC369'>		example, if this variable is &quot;3&quot;, third and after input</div><div class='line' id='LC370'>		characters are fuzzy matched.  But first and second input</div><div class='line' id='LC371'>		characters are not fuzzy matched.</div><div class='line' id='LC372'>		Note: If this variable changed, completion speed may be too</div><div class='line' id='LC373'>		slow.</div><div class='line' id='LC374'><br/></div><div class='line' id='LC375'>		Default value is 3.</div><div class='line' id='LC376'><br/></div><div class='line' id='LC377'>				*g:neocomplcache_enable_caching_message*</div><div class='line' id='LC378'>g:neocomplcache_enable_caching_message</div><div class='line' id='LC379'>		When make cache, this variable controls whether neocomplcache</div><div class='line' id='LC380'>		displays the message in Command-line.</div><div class='line' id='LC381'><br/></div><div class='line' id='LC382'>		Default value is 1.</div><div class='line' id='LC383'><br/></div><div class='line' id='LC384'>				*g:neocomplcache_caching_limit_file_size*</div><div class='line' id='LC385'>g:neocomplcache_caching_limit_file_size</div><div class='line' id='LC386'>		This variable set file size to make a cache of a file.  If</div><div class='line' id='LC387'>		open file is bigger than this size, neocomplcache does not</div><div class='line' id='LC388'>		make a cache.</div><div class='line' id='LC389'><br/></div><div class='line' id='LC390'>		Default value is 500000.</div><div class='line' id='LC391'><br/></div><div class='line' id='LC392'>			*g:neocomplcache_disable_caching_file_path_pattern*</div><div class='line' id='LC393'>g:neocomplcache_disable_caching_file_path_pattern</div><div class='line' id='LC394'>		This variable set a pattern of the buffer file path.  If</div><div class='line' id='LC395'>		matched it, neocomplcache does not save a cache of the buffer.</div><div class='line' id='LC396'>		When it is an empty character string, neocomplcache will</div><div class='line' id='LC397'>		ignore.</div><div class='line' id='LC398'><br/></div><div class='line' id='LC399'>		Default value is &#39;&#39;.</div><div class='line' id='LC400'><br/></div><div class='line' id='LC401'>				*g:neocomplcache_lock_buffer_name_pattern*</div><div class='line' id='LC402'>g:neocomplcache_lock_buffer_name_pattern</div><div class='line' id='LC403'>		This variable set a pattern of the buffer name.  If matched it,</div><div class='line' id='LC404'>		neocomplcache does not complete automatically.  When it is an</div><div class='line' id='LC405'>		empty character string, neocomplcache will ignore.</div><div class='line' id='LC406'><br/></div><div class='line' id='LC407'>		Default value is &#39;&#39;.</div><div class='line' id='LC408'><br/></div><div class='line' id='LC409'>g:neocomplcache_enable_prefetch		*g:neocomplcache_enable_prefetch*</div><div class='line' id='LC410'>		This variable controls whether neocomplcache prefetches.  If</div><div class='line' id='LC411'>		this variable is non-zero, neocomplcache does not flick in</div><div class='line' id='LC412'>		auto completion.</div><div class='line' id='LC413'><br/></div><div class='line' id='LC414'>		Note: This variable has a side effect.  Partial function (ex:</div><div class='line' id='LC415'>		|complete_check()|) is disabled in completefunc.</div><div class='line' id='LC416'>		Note: If this variable is 0, an input problem may occur in</div><div class='line' id='LC417'>		using uim-skk or other IMEs on GVim.</div><div class='line' id='LC418'><br/></div><div class='line' id='LC419'>		Default value is 0 (above or equal to 7.3.519.)</div><div class='line' id='LC420'>		Default value is 1 (|+xim| and GUI version.)</div><div class='line' id='LC421'><br/></div><div class='line' id='LC422'>g:neocomplcache_lock_iminsert		*g:neocomplcache_lock_iminsert*</div><div class='line' id='LC423'>		If this variable is non-zero, neocomplcache locks when</div><div class='line' id='LC424'>		&#39;iminsert&#39; is non-zero.</div><div class='line' id='LC425'><br/></div><div class='line' id='LC426'>		Default value is 0.</div><div class='line' id='LC427'><br/></div><div class='line' id='LC428'>g:neocomplcache_temporary_dir		*g:neocomplcache_temporary_dir*</div><div class='line' id='LC429'>		This variable appoints the directory that neocomplcache</div><div class='line' id='LC430'>		begins to write a file at one time.  When there is not the</div><div class='line' id='LC431'>		directory which appointed here, it is made.  For example,</div><div class='line' id='LC432'>		buffer_complete.vim stores cache of the keyword in this</div><div class='line' id='LC433'>		&#39;buffer_cache&#39; sub directory.</div><div class='line' id='LC434'><br/></div><div class='line' id='LC435'>		Default value is &#39;~/.neocomplcache&#39;.</div><div class='line' id='LC436'><br/></div><div class='line' id='LC437'>g:neocomplcache_keyword_patterns</div><div class='line' id='LC438'>					*g:neocomplcache_keyword_patterns*</div><div class='line' id='LC439'>		This dictionary records keyword patterns to completion.</div><div class='line' id='LC440'>		This is appointed in regular expression every file type.</div><div class='line' id='LC441'>		If the key is &quot;_&quot; or &quot;default&quot;, it is used for default</div><div class='line' id='LC442'>		pattern.</div><div class='line' id='LC443'><br/></div><div class='line' id='LC444'>		Because it is complicated, refer to</div><div class='line' id='LC445'>		neocomplcache#init#_variables() in</div><div class='line' id='LC446'>		autoload/neocomplcache/init.vim for the initial value.</div><div class='line' id='LC447'>&gt;</div><div class='line' id='LC448'>		&quot; Examples:</div><div class='line' id='LC449'>		if !exists(&#39;g:neocomplcache_keyword_patterns&#39;)</div><div class='line' id='LC450'>		  let g:neocomplcache_keyword_patterns = {}</div><div class='line' id='LC451'>		endif</div><div class='line' id='LC452'>		let g:neocomplcache_keyword_patterns._ = &#39;\h\w*&#39;</div><div class='line' id='LC453'>&lt;</div><div class='line' id='LC454'>				*g:neocomplcache_next_keyword_patterns*</div><div class='line' id='LC455'>g:neocomplcache_next_keyword_patterns</div><div class='line' id='LC456'>		This dictionary records regular expression to recognize a</div><div class='line' id='LC457'>		keyword pattern of the next than a cursor.  The form is the</div><div class='line' id='LC458'>		same as |g:neocomplcache_keyword_patterns|.</div><div class='line' id='LC459'><br/></div><div class='line' id='LC460'>		Because it is complicated, refer to</div><div class='line' id='LC461'>		neocomplcache#init#_variables() in</div><div class='line' id='LC462'>		autoload/neocomplcache/init.vim for the initial value.</div><div class='line' id='LC463'><br/></div><div class='line' id='LC464'>g:neocomplcache_omni_patterns		*g:neocomplcache_omni_patterns*</div><div class='line' id='LC465'>		This dictionary records keyword patterns used in</div><div class='line' id='LC466'>		|omni_complete|.  This is appointed in regular expression</div><div class='line' id='LC467'>		every file type or &#39;omnifunc&#39; name.  If this pattern is not</div><div class='line' id='LC468'>		defined or empty pattern, neocomplcache does not call</div><div class='line' id='LC469'>		&#39;omnifunc&#39;.</div><div class='line' id='LC470'>		Note: ruby and php omnifunc are disabled, because they are too</div><div class='line' id='LC471'>		slow.</div><div class='line' id='LC472'>		Note: Partial omnifunc has problem when neocomplcache call(Ex:</div><div class='line' id='LC473'>		rubycomplete, jedi.vim, cocoa.vim and clang_complete).  You should</div><div class='line' id='LC474'>		|g:neocomplcache_force_omni_patterns| instead.</div><div class='line' id='LC475'><br/></div><div class='line' id='LC476'>		Because it is complicated, refer to s:source.initialize()</div><div class='line' id='LC477'>		autoload/neocomplcache/sources/omni_complete.vim for the</div><div class='line' id='LC478'>		initial value.</div><div class='line' id='LC479'>&gt;</div><div class='line' id='LC480'>		&quot; Examples:</div><div class='line' id='LC481'>		if !exists(&#39;g:neocomplcache_omni_patterns&#39;)</div><div class='line' id='LC482'>		let g:neocomplcache_omni_patterns = {}</div><div class='line' id='LC483'>		endif</div><div class='line' id='LC484'>		let g:neocomplcache_omni_patterns.php = &#39;[^. \t]-&gt;\h\w*\|\h\w*::&#39;</div><div class='line' id='LC485'>		let g:neocomplcache_omni_patterns.c = &#39;[^.[:digit:] *\t]\%(\.\|-&gt;\)&#39;</div><div class='line' id='LC486'>		let g:neocomplcache_omni_patterns.cpp = &#39;[^.[:digit:] *\t]\%(\.\|-&gt;\)\|\h\w*::&#39;</div><div class='line' id='LC487'>&lt;</div><div class='line' id='LC488'>					*g:neocomplcache_force_omni_patterns*</div><div class='line' id='LC489'>g:neocomplcache_force_omni_patterns</div><div class='line' id='LC490'>		This dictionary records keyword patterns to Omni completion.</div><div class='line' id='LC491'>		This is appointed in regular expression every file type.</div><div class='line' id='LC492'>		If this pattern is not defined or empty pattern, neocomplcache</div><div class='line' id='LC493'>		does not call &#39;omnifunc&#39;.</div><div class='line' id='LC494'>		Note: If it is a set, neocomplcache will call &#39;omnifunc&#39; or</div><div class='line' id='LC495'>		|g:neocomplcache_omni_functions| directly.  So almost</div><div class='line' id='LC496'>		neocomplcache features are disabled.  But all Omni completion</div><div class='line' id='LC497'>		works instead of |g:neocomplcache_omni_patterns|.</div><div class='line' id='LC498'>		Note: This feature may change &#39;omnifunc&#39; value.</div><div class='line' id='LC499'>&gt;</div><div class='line' id='LC500'>		if !exists(&#39;g:neocomplcache_force_omni_patterns&#39;)</div><div class='line' id='LC501'>		  let g:neocomplcache_force_omni_patterns = {}</div><div class='line' id='LC502'>		endif</div><div class='line' id='LC503'>		let g:neocomplcache_force_omni_patterns.ruby = &#39;[^. *\t]\.\w*\|\h\w*::&#39;</div><div class='line' id='LC504'>&lt;</div><div class='line' id='LC505'>		Because it is complicated, refer to</div><div class='line' id='LC506'>		neocomplcache#init#_variables() in</div><div class='line' id='LC507'>		autoload/neocomplcache/init.vim for the initial value.</div><div class='line' id='LC508'><br/></div><div class='line' id='LC509'>					*g:neocomplcache_tags_filter_patterns*</div><div class='line' id='LC510'>g:neocomplcache_tags_filter_patterns</div><div class='line' id='LC511'>		This dictionary records a pattern to filter a candidate in</div><div class='line' id='LC512'>		the tag completion.  For example, it can exclude a candidate</div><div class='line' id='LC513'>		beginning in _ in file type of C/C++.</div><div class='line' id='LC514'><br/></div><div class='line' id='LC515'>		Because it is complicated, refer to</div><div class='line' id='LC516'>		neocomplcache#init#_variables() in</div><div class='line' id='LC517'>		autoload/neocomplcache/init.vim for the initial value.</div><div class='line' id='LC518'><br/></div><div class='line' id='LC519'>				*g:neocomplcache_tags_caching_limit_file_size*</div><div class='line' id='LC520'>g:neocomplcache_tags_caching_limit_file_size</div><div class='line' id='LC521'>		This variable set file size to make a cache of a file in</div><div class='line' id='LC522'>		tags_complete source.  If open file is bigger than this size,</div><div class='line' id='LC523'>		neocomplcache does not make a tags cache.</div><div class='line' id='LC524'><br/></div><div class='line' id='LC525'>		Default value is 500000.</div><div class='line' id='LC526'><br/></div><div class='line' id='LC527'>				*g:neocomplcache_same_filetype_lists*</div><div class='line' id='LC528'>g:neocomplcache_same_filetype_lists</div><div class='line' id='LC529'>		It is a dictionary to connect file type mutually.  It is</div><div class='line' id='LC530'>		effective at time to let you refer to c and cpp mutually.</div><div class='line' id='LC531'>		The value are comma-separated filetypes.</div><div class='line' id='LC532'>		If the value contains &quot;_&quot;, neocomplcache completes from all</div><div class='line' id='LC533'>		buffers.  If the key is &quot;_&quot;, the value will be used for default</div><div class='line' id='LC534'>		same filetypes.</div><div class='line' id='LC535'>		Note: neocomplcache completes from same filetype buffers in</div><div class='line' id='LC536'>		default.</div><div class='line' id='LC537'>&gt;</div><div class='line' id='LC538'>		if !exists(&#39;g:neocomplcache_same_filetype_lists&#39;)</div><div class='line' id='LC539'>		  let g:neocomplcache_same_filetype_lists = {}</div><div class='line' id='LC540'>		endif</div><div class='line' id='LC541'>		&quot; In c buffers, completes from cpp and d buffers.</div><div class='line' id='LC542'>		let g:neocomplcache_same_filetype_lists.c = &#39;cpp,d&#39;</div><div class='line' id='LC543'>		&quot; In cpp buffers, completes from c buffers.</div><div class='line' id='LC544'>		let g:neocomplcache_same_filetype_lists.cpp = &#39;c&#39;</div><div class='line' id='LC545'>		&quot; In gitconfig buffers, completes from all buffers.</div><div class='line' id='LC546'>		let g:neocomplcache_same_filetype_lists.gitconfig = &#39;_&#39;</div><div class='line' id='LC547'>		&quot; In default, completes from all buffers.</div><div class='line' id='LC548'>		let g:neocomplcache_same_filetype_lists._ = &#39;_&#39;</div><div class='line' id='LC549'>&lt;</div><div class='line' id='LC550'>		Because it is complicated, refer to</div><div class='line' id='LC551'>		neocomplcache#init#_variables() in</div><div class='line' id='LC552'>		autoload/neocomplcache/init.vim for the initial value.</div><div class='line' id='LC553'>		Note: To disable neocomplcache initialization, you must use</div><div class='line' id='LC554'>		|neocomplcache#disable_default_dictionary()|.</div><div class='line' id='LC555'><br/></div><div class='line' id='LC556'>				*g:neocomplcache_dictionary_filetype_lists*</div><div class='line' id='LC557'>g:neocomplcache_dictionary_filetype_lists</div><div class='line' id='LC558'>		It is a dictionary to connect a dictionary file with file</div><div class='line' id='LC559'>		type.  The dictionary&#39;s key is filetype and comma-separated</div><div class='line' id='LC560'>		multiple value is a path to a dictionary file.  If this</div><div class='line' id='LC561'>		variable is empty, neocomplcache uses &#39;dictionary&#39; option.</div><div class='line' id='LC562'>		When you set &quot;text&quot; key, you will appoint dictionary files in</div><div class='line' id='LC563'>		text mode.</div><div class='line' id='LC564'>		Note: Global &#39;dictionary&#39; file is not loaded automatically.</div><div class='line' id='LC565'><br/></div><div class='line' id='LC566'>		Default value is {}.</div><div class='line' id='LC567'><br/></div><div class='line' id='LC568'>					*g:neocomplcache_dictionary_patterns*</div><div class='line' id='LC569'>g:neocomplcache_dictionary_patterns</div><div class='line' id='LC570'>		It is a dictionary to dictionary keyword patterns.  The</div><div class='line' id='LC571'>		dictionary&#39;s key is filetype and value is keyword pattern.</div><div class='line' id='LC572'>		If this variable is empty, neocomplcache uses</div><div class='line' id='LC573'>		|g:neocomplcache_keyword_patterns| option.</div><div class='line' id='LC574'><br/></div><div class='line' id='LC575'>		Default value is {}.</div><div class='line' id='LC576'><br/></div><div class='line' id='LC577'>				*g:neocomplcache_context_filetype_lists*</div><div class='line' id='LC578'>g:neocomplcache_context_filetype_lists</div><div class='line' id='LC579'>		It is a dictionary to define context filetypes.</div><div class='line' id='LC580'>		The item is a list of dictionaries.</div><div class='line' id='LC581'>				*g:neocomplcache_filetype_include_lists*</div><div class='line' id='LC582'>		Note: g:neocomplcache_filetype_include_lists is deprecated</div><div class='line' id='LC583'>		name.</div><div class='line' id='LC584'><br/></div><div class='line' id='LC585'>		The keys and values are below.</div><div class='line' id='LC586'>		&quot;filetype&quot; : includes filetype name.</div><div class='line' id='LC587'>		&quot;start&quot; : filetype start pattern.</div><div class='line' id='LC588'>		&quot;end&quot; : filetype end pattern.  You can use \1 to refer start&#39;s</div><div class='line' id='LC589'>			matched pattern.</div><div class='line' id='LC590'>&gt;</div><div class='line' id='LC591'>		&quot; Examples:</div><div class='line' id='LC592'>		if !exists(&#39;g:neocomplcache_context_filetype_lists&#39;)</div><div class='line' id='LC593'>		let g:neocomplcache_context_filetype_lists = {}</div><div class='line' id='LC594'>		endif</div><div class='line' id='LC595'>		let g:neocomplcache_context_filetype_lists.perl6 =</div><div class='line' id='LC596'>		\ [{&#39;filetype&#39; : &#39;pir&#39;, &#39;start&#39; : &#39;Q:PIR\s*{&#39;, &#39;end&#39; : &#39;}&#39;}]</div><div class='line' id='LC597'>		let g:neocomplcache_context_filetype_lists.vim =</div><div class='line' id='LC598'>		\ [{&#39;filetype&#39; : &#39;python&#39;, &#39;start&#39; : &#39;^\s*python &lt;&lt;\s*\(\h\w*\)&#39;, &#39;end&#39; : &#39;^\1&#39;}]</div><div class='line' id='LC599'>&lt;</div><div class='line' id='LC600'>		Because it is complicated, refer to</div><div class='line' id='LC601'>		neocomplcache#init#_variables() in</div><div class='line' id='LC602'>		autoload/neocomplcache/init.vim for the initial value.</div><div class='line' id='LC603'><br/></div><div class='line' id='LC604'>					*g:neocomplcache_text_mode_filetypes*</div><div class='line' id='LC605'>g:neocomplcache_text_mode_filetypes</div><div class='line' id='LC606'>		It is a dictionary to define text mode filetypes.  The</div><div class='line' id='LC607'>		dictionary&#39;s key is filetype and value is number.  If the</div><div class='line' id='LC608'>		value is non-zero, this filetype is text mode.  In text mode,</div><div class='line' id='LC609'>		neocomplcache supports word conversion to write English.</div><div class='line' id='LC610'><br/></div><div class='line' id='LC611'>		For example, if you input &quot;Fo&quot;, neocomplcache will convert</div><div class='line' id='LC612'>		candidate &quot;foo&quot; to &quot;Foo&quot;.  If you input &quot;foo&quot;, neocomplcache</div><div class='line' id='LC613'>		will convert candidate &quot;FooBar&quot; to &quot;foobar&quot;.  If you input</div><div class='line' id='LC614'>		&quot;FO&quot;, neocomplcache will convert candidate &quot;foo&quot; to &quot;FOO&quot;.</div><div class='line' id='LC615'>		Note: Text mode conversion is only used for &quot;foobar&quot; or</div><div class='line' id='LC616'>		&quot;Foobar&quot; or &quot;FOOBAR&quot; words.  Not &quot;fooBar&quot; or &quot;FooBar&quot;.</div><div class='line' id='LC617'><br/></div><div class='line' id='LC618'>		Because it is complicated, refer to</div><div class='line' id='LC619'>		neocomplcache#init#_variables() in</div><div class='line' id='LC620'>		autoload/neocomplcache/init.vim for the initial value.</div><div class='line' id='LC621'><br/></div><div class='line' id='LC622'>g:neocomplcache_ctags_program		*g:neocomplcache_ctags_program*</div><div class='line' id='LC623'>		It is the path to the ctags command.  If this command is not</div><div class='line' id='LC624'>		installed, include_complete is disabled.</div><div class='line' id='LC625'><br/></div><div class='line' id='LC626'>		Default value is &quot;ctags&quot;.</div><div class='line' id='LC627'><br/></div><div class='line' id='LC628'>g:neocomplcache_ctags_arguments_list</div><div class='line' id='LC629'>					*g:neocomplcache_ctags_arguments_list*</div><div class='line' id='LC630'>		It is the dictionary of the character string to set a value</div><div class='line' id='LC631'>		to give as an argument of the commands when buffer_complete</div><div class='line' id='LC632'>		and include_complete use a ctags command.  The dictionary&#39;s</div><div class='line' id='LC633'>		key is filetype.  If the key is &quot;_&quot;, it will be used for</div><div class='line' id='LC634'>		default.</div><div class='line' id='LC635'><br/></div><div class='line' id='LC636'>		Because it is complicated, refer to</div><div class='line' id='LC637'>		neocomplcache#init#_variables() in</div><div class='line' id='LC638'>		autoload/neocomplcache/init.vim for the initial value.</div><div class='line' id='LC639'><br/></div><div class='line' id='LC640'>g:neocomplcache_include_paths		*g:neocomplcache_include_paths*</div><div class='line' id='LC641'>		It is the variable to enumerate path of the include file</div><div class='line' id='LC642'>		every file type.  When there is not it, &#39;path&#39; is used.</div><div class='line' id='LC643'>		Refer to &#39;path&#39; for the description form.  It is the</div><div class='line' id='LC644'>		dictionary of the character string that assumed file type a</div><div class='line' id='LC645'>		key.</div><div class='line' id='LC646'><br/></div><div class='line' id='LC647'>		Because it is complicated, refer to s:source.initialize() in</div><div class='line' id='LC648'>		autoload/neocomplcache/sources/include_complete.vim for the</div><div class='line' id='LC649'>		initial value.</div><div class='line' id='LC650'><br/></div><div class='line' id='LC651'>g:neocomplcache_include_exprs			*g:neocomplcache_include_exprs*</div><div class='line' id='LC652'>		It is the expression string of the line analysis to perform</div><div class='line' id='LC653'>		to acquire an include file name.  When there is not it,</div><div class='line' id='LC654'>		&#39;includeexpr&#39; is used.  Refer to &#39;includeexpr&#39; for the</div><div class='line' id='LC655'>		description form.  It is the dictionary of the character</div><div class='line' id='LC656'>		string that assumed file type a key.</div><div class='line' id='LC657'><br/></div><div class='line' id='LC658'>		Because it is complicated, refer to s:source.initialize() in</div><div class='line' id='LC659'>		autoload/neocomplcache/sources/include_complete.vim for the</div><div class='line' id='LC660'>		initial value.</div><div class='line' id='LC661'><br/></div><div class='line' id='LC662'>g:neocomplcache_include_patterns	*g:neocomplcache_include_patterns*</div><div class='line' id='LC663'>		This variable appoints the pattern of the include command.</div><div class='line' id='LC664'>		When there is not it, &#39;include&#39; is used.  Refer to &#39;include&#39;</div><div class='line' id='LC665'>		for the description form.  It is the dictionary of the</div><div class='line' id='LC666'>		character string that assumed file type a key.</div><div class='line' id='LC667'><br/></div><div class='line' id='LC668'>		Because it is complicated, refer to s:source.initialize() in</div><div class='line' id='LC669'>		autoload/neocomplcache/sources/include_complete.vim for the</div><div class='line' id='LC670'>		initial value.</div><div class='line' id='LC671'><br/></div><div class='line' id='LC672'>					*g:neocomplcache_include_functions*</div><div class='line' id='LC673'>g:neocomplcache_include_functions</div><div class='line' id='LC674'>		This variable appoints the function name of the include</div><div class='line' id='LC675'>		command.  When there is not it, ignored.  It is the dictionary</div><div class='line' id='LC676'>		of the function name string that assumed file type a key.</div><div class='line' id='LC677'><br/></div><div class='line' id='LC678'>		The function args are {lines} and {path}.</div><div class='line' id='LC679'>		{lines} is the list of buffer lines.</div><div class='line' id='LC680'>		{path} is the include path.</div><div class='line' id='LC681'>		The return value is the list of include files.</div><div class='line' id='LC682'><br/></div><div class='line' id='LC683'>		Because it is complicated, refer to s:source.initialize() in</div><div class='line' id='LC684'>		autoload/neocomplcache/sources/include_complete.vim for the</div><div class='line' id='LC685'>		initial value.</div><div class='line' id='LC686'><br/></div><div class='line' id='LC687'>				*g:neocomplcache_include_max_processes*</div><div class='line' id='LC688'>g:neocomplcache_include_max_processes</div><div class='line' id='LC689'>		This variable appoints the max number of include processes.</div><div class='line' id='LC690'>		When this variable is 0, include process will be disabled.</div><div class='line' id='LC691'><br/></div><div class='line' id='LC692'>		Default value is 20.</div><div class='line' id='LC693'><br/></div><div class='line' id='LC694'>				*g:neocomplcache_filename_include_exprs*</div><div class='line' id='LC695'>g:neocomplcache_filename_include_exprs</div><div class='line' id='LC696'>		It is the expression string of the line analysis to perform</div><div class='line' id='LC697'>		to substitute an include file name.  When there is not it,</div><div class='line' id='LC698'>		ignored.  Refer to &#39;includeexpr&#39; for the</div><div class='line' id='LC699'>		description form.  It is the dictionary of the character</div><div class='line' id='LC700'>		string that assumed file type a key.</div><div class='line' id='LC701'><br/></div><div class='line' id='LC702'>		Example: Perl</div><div class='line' id='LC703'>&gt;</div><div class='line' id='LC704'>		let g:neocomplcache_filename_include_exprs.perl =</div><div class='line' id='LC705'>		\ &#39;fnamemodify(substitute(v:fname, &quot;/&quot;, &quot;::&quot;, &quot;g&quot;), &quot;:r&quot;)&#39;</div><div class='line' id='LC706'>&lt;</div><div class='line' id='LC707'><br/></div><div class='line' id='LC708'>		Because it is complicated, refer to s:source.initialize() in</div><div class='line' id='LC709'>		autoload/neocomplcache/sources/filename_complete.vim for the</div><div class='line' id='LC710'>		initial value.</div><div class='line' id='LC711'><br/></div><div class='line' id='LC712'>				*g:neocomplcache_filename_include_exts*</div><div class='line' id='LC713'>g:neocomplcache_filename_include_exts</div><div class='line' id='LC714'>		It is the list of include file name extensions.  When there</div><div class='line' id='LC715'>		is not it, all file name is used.  It is the dictionary of</div><div class='line' id='LC716'>		the list that assumed file type a key.</div><div class='line' id='LC717'><br/></div><div class='line' id='LC718'>		Example: C++</div><div class='line' id='LC719'>&gt;</div><div class='line' id='LC720'>		let g:neocomplcache_filename_include_exts.cpp =</div><div class='line' id='LC721'>		\ [&#39;&#39;, &#39;h&#39;, &#39;hpp&#39;, &#39;hxx&#39;]</div><div class='line' id='LC722'>&lt;</div><div class='line' id='LC723'>		Because it is complicated, refer to s:source.initialize() in</div><div class='line' id='LC724'>		autoload/neocomplcache/sources/filename_complete.vim for the</div><div class='line' id='LC725'>		initial value.</div><div class='line' id='LC726'><br/></div><div class='line' id='LC727'>				*g:neocomplcache_member_prefix_patterns*</div><div class='line' id='LC728'>g:neocomplcache_member_prefix_patterns</div><div class='line' id='LC729'>		This variable appoints a prefix pattern to complete a member</div><div class='line' id='LC730'>		in buffer_complete.</div><div class='line' id='LC731'>		This is appointed in regular expression every file type.</div><div class='line' id='LC732'>		If filetype key is not set, disable member completion.</div><div class='line' id='LC733'><br/></div><div class='line' id='LC734'>		Because it is complicated, refer in</div><div class='line' id='LC735'>		autoload/neocomplcache/sources/buffer_complete.vim for the</div><div class='line' id='LC736'>		initial value.</div><div class='line' id='LC737'><br/></div><div class='line' id='LC738'>g:neocomplcache_member_patterns		*g:neocomplcache_member_patterns*</div><div class='line' id='LC739'>		This variable appoints a keyword pattern to complete a member</div><div class='line' id='LC740'>		in buffer_complete.</div><div class='line' id='LC741'>		This is appointed in regular expression every file type.</div><div class='line' id='LC742'>		If filetype key is not set, use filetype &quot;default&quot; setting.</div><div class='line' id='LC743'><br/></div><div class='line' id='LC744'>		Because it is complicated, refer in</div><div class='line' id='LC745'>		autoload/neocomplcache/sources/buffer_complete.vim for the</div><div class='line' id='LC746'>		initial value.</div><div class='line' id='LC747'><br/></div><div class='line' id='LC748'>					*g:neocomplcache_delimiter_patterns*</div><div class='line' id='LC749'>g:neocomplcache_delimiter_patterns</div><div class='line' id='LC750'>		This variable appoints a delimiter pattern to smart complete a</div><div class='line' id='LC751'>		function.  This is appointed in regular expression&#39;s string</div><div class='line' id='LC752'>		list every file type.</div><div class='line' id='LC753'>&gt;</div><div class='line' id='LC754'>		&quot; Examples:</div><div class='line' id='LC755'>		if !exists(&#39;g:neocomplcache_delimiter_patterns&#39;)</div><div class='line' id='LC756'>		let g:neocomplcache_delimiter_patterns= {}</div><div class='line' id='LC757'>		endif</div><div class='line' id='LC758'>		let g:neocomplcache_delimiter_patterns.vim = [&#39;#&#39;]</div><div class='line' id='LC759'>		let g:neocomplcache_delimiter_patterns.cpp = [&#39;::&#39;]</div><div class='line' id='LC760'>&lt;</div><div class='line' id='LC761'>		Because it is complicated, refer to</div><div class='line' id='LC762'>		neocomplcache#init#_variables() in</div><div class='line' id='LC763'>		autoload/neocomplcache/init.vim for the initial value.</div><div class='line' id='LC764'><br/></div><div class='line' id='LC765'>g:neocomplcache_omni_functions		*g:neocomplcache_omni_functions*</div><div class='line' id='LC766'>		This dictionary which appoints |omni_complete| call functions.</div><div class='line' id='LC767'>		The key is |&amp;filetype|.  The value is omnifunc String or List</div><div class='line' id='LC768'>		of omnifunc String.  If</div><div class='line' id='LC769'>		g:neocomplcache_omni_function_list[|&amp;filetype|] is undefined,</div><div class='line' id='LC770'>		|omni_complete| calls |omnifunc|.</div><div class='line' id='LC771'>		If the key is &quot;_&quot;, used for all filetypes.</div><div class='line' id='LC772'><br/></div><div class='line' id='LC773'>		Default value is {}.</div><div class='line' id='LC774'><br/></div><div class='line' id='LC775'>					*g:neocomplcache_vim_completefuncs*</div><div class='line' id='LC776'>g:neocomplcache_vim_completefuncs</div><div class='line' id='LC777'>		This dictionary which appoints |vim_complete| call function</div><div class='line' id='LC778'>		when completes custom and customlist command.  The key is</div><div class='line' id='LC779'>		command name.  The value is function name.</div><div class='line' id='LC780'><br/></div><div class='line' id='LC781'>		Default value is {}.</div><div class='line' id='LC782'>&gt;</div><div class='line' id='LC783'>		&quot; Examples:</div><div class='line' id='LC784'>		if !exists(&#39;g:neocomplcache_vim_completefuncs&#39;)</div><div class='line' id='LC785'>		  let g:neocomplcache_vim_completefuncs = {}</div><div class='line' id='LC786'>		endif</div><div class='line' id='LC787'>		let g:neocomplcache_vim_completefuncs.Ref = &#39;ref#complete&#39;</div><div class='line' id='LC788'>&lt;</div><div class='line' id='LC789'>					*g:neocomplcache_sources_list*</div><div class='line' id='LC790'>g:neocomplcache_sources_list</div><div class='line' id='LC791'>		It is a dictionary to decide use source names.  The key is</div><div class='line' id='LC792'>		filetype and the value is source names list.  If the key is</div><div class='line' id='LC793'>		&quot;_&quot;, the value will be used for default filetypes.  For</div><div class='line' id='LC794'>		example, you can disable some sources in C++ filetype.</div><div class='line' id='LC795'>		If the value is &quot;_&quot;, it will load all sources.</div><div class='line' id='LC796'>		Default value is {}.</div><div class='line' id='LC797'>&gt;</div><div class='line' id='LC798'>		&quot; Examples:</div><div class='line' id='LC799'>		if !exists(&#39;g:neocomplcache_sources_list&#39;)</div><div class='line' id='LC800'>		  let g:neocomplcache_sources_list = {}</div><div class='line' id='LC801'>		endif</div><div class='line' id='LC802'>		let g:neocomplcache_sources_list._ = [&#39;buffer_complete&#39;]</div><div class='line' id='LC803'>		let g:neocomplcache_sources_list.cpp =</div><div class='line' id='LC804'>		\ [&#39;buffer_complete&#39;, &#39;include_complete&#39;]</div><div class='line' id='LC805'>&lt;</div><div class='line' id='LC806'>					*b:neocomplcache_sources_list*</div><div class='line' id='LC807'>b:neocomplcache_sources_list</div><div class='line' id='LC808'>		It is a list to decide use source names in buffer local.</div><div class='line' id='LC809'>&gt;</div><div class='line' id='LC810'>		&quot; Examples:</div><div class='line' id='LC811'>		&quot; In cmdwin, only use vim_complete source.</div><div class='line' id='LC812'>		autocmd CmdwinEnter * let b:neocomplcache_sources_list = [&#39;vim_complete&#39;]</div><div class='line' id='LC813'>&lt;</div><div class='line' id='LC814'>				*g:neocomplcache_disabled_sources_list*</div><div class='line' id='LC815'>g:neocomplcache_disabled_sources_list</div><div class='line' id='LC816'>		It is a dictionary to decide disabled source names.  The key is</div><div class='line' id='LC817'>		filetype and the value is source names list.  If the key is</div><div class='line' id='LC818'>		&quot;_&quot;, the value will be used for default filetypes.</div><div class='line' id='LC819'>		If the value is &quot;_&quot;, it will load all sources.</div><div class='line' id='LC820'>		Default value is {}.</div><div class='line' id='LC821'>&gt;</div><div class='line' id='LC822'>		&quot; Examples:</div><div class='line' id='LC823'>		if !exists(&#39;g:neocomplcache_disabled_sources_list&#39;)</div><div class='line' id='LC824'>		  let g:neocomplcache_disabled_sources_list = {}</div><div class='line' id='LC825'>		endif</div><div class='line' id='LC826'>		&quot; Disable dictionary_complete in python filetype.</div><div class='line' id='LC827'>		let g:neocomplcache_disabled_sources_list.python =</div><div class='line' id='LC828'>		\ [&#39;dictionary_complete&#39;]</div><div class='line' id='LC829'>&lt;</div><div class='line' id='LC830'>					*g:neocomplcache_source_disable*</div><div class='line' id='LC831'>		Note: g:neocomplcache_source_disable is deprecated variable.</div><div class='line' id='LC832'>		Default value is {}.</div><div class='line' id='LC833'><br/></div><div class='line' id='LC834'>				*g:neocomplcache_source_completion_length*</div><div class='line' id='LC835'>g:neocomplcache_source_completion_length</div><div class='line' id='LC836'>		Note: This option is deprecated. You should use</div><div class='line' id='LC845'>		|neocomplcache#custom_source()| instead of it.</div><div class='line' id='LC846'>&gt;</div><div class='line' id='LC847'>		&quot; Examples:</div><div class='line' id='LC848'>		call neocomplcache#custom_source(</div><div class='line' id='LC849'>				\ &#39;buffer_complete&#39;, &#39;rank&#39;, 10)</div><div class='line' id='LC850'>&lt;</div><div class='line' id='LC851'>		The default rank of each sources:</div><div class='line' id='LC852'>		filename_complete : 3</div><div class='line' id='LC853'>		dictionary_complete : 4</div><div class='line' id='LC854'>		buffer_complete : 5</div><div class='line' id='LC855'>		syntax_complete : 4</div><div class='line' id='LC856'>		include_complete : 8</div><div class='line' id='LC857'>		snippets_complete : 8</div><div class='line' id='LC858'>		vim_complete : 100</div><div class='line' id='LC859'>		omni_complete : 50</div><div class='line' id='LC860'>		other keyword sources : 5</div><div class='line' id='LC861'>		other manual sources : 10</div><div class='line' id='LC862'>		other manual sources with filetype : 100</div><div class='line' id='LC863'><br/></div><div class='line' id='LC864'>				*g:neocomplcache_force_overwrite_completefunc*</div><div class='line' id='LC865'>g:neocomplcache_force_overwrite_completefunc</div><div class='line' id='LC866'>		If this variable is 1, neocomplcache forces overwrite</div><div class='line' id='LC867'>		&#39;completefunc&#39; option. But other plugin&#39;s</div><div class='line' id='LC869'>		&#39;completefunc&#39; is disabled.</div><div class='line' id='LC870'><br/></div><div class='line' id='LC871'>		Default value is 0.</div><div class='line' id='LC872'><br/></div><div class='line' id='LC873'>					*g:neocomplcache_release_cache_time*</div><div class='line' id='LC874'>g:neocomplcache_release_cache_time</div><div class='line' id='LC875'>		This variable defines time of automatic released cache by a</div><div class='line' id='LC876'>		second unit.</div><div class='line' id='LC877'><br/></div><div class='line' id='LC878'>		Default value is 900.</div><div class='line' id='LC879'><br/></div><div class='line' id='LC880'>g:neocomplcache_use_vimproc			*g:neocomplcache_use_vimproc*</div><div class='line' id='LC881'>		This variable is non 0, neocomplcache uses |vimproc|.</div><div class='line' id='LC882'>		Note: If this variable is non 0, neocomplcache will make cache</div><div class='line' id='LC883'>		asynchronously.</div><div class='line' id='LC884'><br/></div><div class='line' id='LC885'>		Default value is vimproc auto detection result.</div><div class='line' id='LC886'><br/></div><div class='line' id='LC887'>			*g:neocomplcache_ignore_composite_filetype_lists*</div><div class='line' id='LC888'>g:neocomplcache_ignore_composite_filetype_lists</div><div class='line' id='LC889'>		It is a dictionary to ignore composite file type.</div><div class='line' id='LC890'>		The dictionary&#39;s key is composite filetype and value is</div><div class='line' id='LC891'>		filetype.</div><div class='line' id='LC892'>&gt;</div><div class='line' id='LC893'>		&quot; Examples:</div><div class='line' id='LC894'>		let g:neocomplcache_ignore_composite_filetype_lists = {</div><div class='line' id='LC895'>			\ &#39;ruby.spec&#39; : &#39;ruby&#39;</div><div class='line' id='LC896'>			\ }</div><div class='line' id='LC897'>&lt;</div><div class='line' id='LC898'>		If you open filetype like |ruby.spec|, completion is</div><div class='line' id='LC899'>		intended for |ruby| and |spec|.</div><div class='line' id='LC900'>		But if you only want to complete |ruby| filetype,</div><div class='line' id='LC901'>		you can set this variable to ignore |spec|.</div><div class='line' id='LC902'><br/></div><div class='line' id='LC903'>		Default value is {}.</div><div class='line' id='LC904'><br/></div><div class='line' id='LC905'>					*g:neocomplcache_wildcard_characters*</div><div class='line' id='LC906'>g:neocomplcache_wildcard_characters</div><div class='line' id='LC907'>		It is a dictionary to define wildcard characters.</div><div class='line' id='LC908'>		You can change default wildcard character &quot;*&quot; character.</div><div class='line' id='LC914'>&gt;</div><div class='line' id='LC915'>		&quot; Examples:</div><div class='line' id='LC916'>		if !exists(&#39;g:neocomplcache_wildcard_characters&#39;)</div><div class='line' id='LC917'>		  let g:neocomplcache_wildcard_characters = {}</div><div class='line' id='LC918'>		endif</div><div &#39;*&#39; }.</div><div class='line' id='LC922'><br/></div><div class='line' id='LC923'>				*g:neocomplcache_skip_auto_completion_time*</div><div class='line' id='LC924'>g:neocomplcache_skip_auto_completion_time</div><div class='line' id='LC925'>		It is a string for skip auto completion.</div><div class='line' id='LC926'>		If completion time is higher than it, neocomplcache will skip</div><div class='line' id='LC927'>		auto completion.</div><div class='line' id='LC928'>		If it is &quot;&quot;, the skip feature will be disabled.</div><div class='line' id='LC929'><br/></div><div class='line' id='LC930'>		Default value is &quot;0.3&quot;.</div><div class='line' id='LC931'>		{only available when compiled with the |+reltime| feature}</div><div class='line' id='LC932'><br/></div><div class='line' id='LC933'>				*g:neocomplcache_enable_auto_close_preview*</div><div class='line' id='LC934'>g:neocomplcache_enable_auto_close_preview</div><div class='line' id='LC935'>		If it is non-zero, neocomplcache will close preview window</div><div class='line' id='LC936'>		automatically.</div><div class='line' id='LC937'><br/></div><div class='line' id='LC938'>		Default value is 1.</div><div class='line' id='LC939'><br/></div><div class='line' id='LC940'>------------------------------------------------------------------------------</div><div class='line' id='LC941'>FUNCTIONS 					*neocomplcache-functions*</div><div class='line' id='LC942'><br/></div><div class='line' id='LC943'>neocomplcache#initialize()			*neocomplcache#initialize()*</div><div class='line' id='LC944'>		Initialize neocomplcache and sources.</div><div class='line' id='LC945'>		Note: It enables neocomplcache.</div><div class='line' id='LC946'>		Note: You should call it in |VimEnter| autocmd.</div><div class='line' id='LC947'>		User customization for neocomplcache must be set before</div><div class='line' id='LC948'>		initialization of neocomplcache.</div><div class='line' id='LC949'><br/></div><div class='line' id='LC950'>neocomplcache#custom_source({source-name}, {option-name}, {value})</div><div class='line' id='LC951'>						*neocomplcache#custom_source()*</div><div class='line' id='LC952'>		Set {source-name} source specialized {option-name}</div><div class='line' id='LC953'>		to {value}. You may specify multiple sources with</div><div class='line' id='LC954'>		separating &quot;,&quot; in {source-name}.</div><div class='line' id='LC955'>		If {source-name} is &quot;_&quot;, sources default option will be</div><div class='line' id='LC956'>		change.</div><div class='line' id='LC957'><br/></div><div class='line' id='LC958'>		These options below are available:</div><div class='line' id='LC959'>		|neocomplcache-source-attributes|</div><div class='line' id='LC960'>		Note: User customization for neocomplcache must be set before</div><div class='line' id='LC961'>		initialization of neocomplcache.</div><div class='line' id='LC962'><br/></div><div class='line' id='LC963'>					*neocomplcache#get_context_filetype()*</div><div class='line' id='LC964'>neocomplcache#get_context_filetype()</div><div class='line' id='LC965'>		Get current context filetype of the cursor.  This is smarter</div><div class='line' id='LC966'>		than |&amp;filetype| about handling nested filetypes.</div><div class='line' id='LC967'><br/></div><div class='line' id='LC968'>		For example html filetype has javascript inside.  Say, you have</div><div class='line' id='LC969'>		a buffer which content is below with filetype is html.</div><div class='line' id='LC970'>&gt;</div><div class='line' id='LC971'>		&lt;script type=&quot;text/javascript&quot;&gt;</div><div class='line' id='LC972'>		  var x = 1;</div><div class='line' id='LC973'>		&lt;/script&gt;</div><div class='line' id='LC974'>&lt;</div><div class='line' id='LC975'>		At the line 1 and 3, neocomplcache#get_context_filetype() is</div><div class='line' id='LC976'>		&quot;html&quot; and at the line 2 it&#39;s &quot;javascript&quot;, whilst at any</div><div class='line' id='LC977'>		lines &amp;filetype is &quot;html&quot;.</div><div class='line' id='LC978'><br/></div><div class='line' id='LC979'>				*neocomplcache#disable_default_dictionary()*</div><div class='line' id='LC980'>neocomplcache#disable_default_dictionary({variable-name})</div><div class='line' id='LC981'>		Disable default {variable-name} dictionary initialization.</div><div class='line' id='LC982'>		Note: It must be called in .vimrc.</div><div class='line' id='LC983'>&gt;</div><div class='line' id='LC984'>	call neocomplcache#disable_default_dictionary(</div><div class='line' id='LC985'>	      \ &#39;g:neocomplcache_same_filetype_lists&#39;)</div><div class='line' id='LC986'>&lt;</div><div class='line' id='LC987'>------------------------------------------------------------------------------</div><div class='line' id='LC988'>KEY MAPPINGS 					*neocomplcache-key-mappings*</div><div class='line' id='LC989'><br/></div><div class='line' id='LC990'>				*neocomplcache#start_manual_complete()*</div><div class='line' id='LC991'>neocomplcache#start_manual_complete([{sources}])</div><div class='line' id='LC992'>		Use this function on inoremap &lt;expr&gt;.  The keymapping call the</div><div class='line' id='LC993'>		completion of neocomplcache.  When you rearrange the completion</div><div class='line' id='LC994'>		of the Vim standard, you use it.</div><div class='line' id='LC995'>		If you give {sources} argument, neocomplcache call {sources}.</div><div class='line' id='LC996'>		{sources} is name of source or list of sources name.</div><div class='line' id='LC997'>&gt;</div><div class='line' id='LC998'>		inoremap &lt;expr&gt;&lt;Tab&gt;  neocomplcache#start_manual_complete()</div><div class='line' id='LC999'>&lt;</div><div class='line' id='LC1000'>				*neocomplcache#manual_filename_complete()*</div><div class='line' id='LC1001'>				*neocomplcache#manual_omni_complete()*</div><div class='line' id='LC1002'>		Note: These functions are obsolete.</div><div class='line' id='LC1003'><br/></div><div class='line' id='LC1004'>				*neocomplcache#close_popup()*</div><div class='line' id='LC1005'>neocomplcache#close_popup()</div><div class='line' id='LC1006'>		Inset candidate and close popup menu for neocomplcache.</div><div class='line' id='LC1007'>&gt;</div><div class='line' id='LC1008'>		inoremap &lt;expr&gt;&lt;C-y&gt;  neocomplcache#close_popup()</div><div class='line' id='LC1009'>&lt;</div><div class='line' id='LC1010'>				*neocomplcache#cancel_popup()*</div><div class='line' id='LC1011'>neocomplcache#cancel_popup()</div><div class='line' id='LC1012'>		cancel completion menu for neocomplcache.</div><div class='line' id='LC1013'>&gt;</div><div class='line' id='LC1014'>		inoremap &lt;expr&gt;&lt;C-e&gt;
