Because tags_complete is</div><div class='line' id='LC1170'>		too slow if tags_complete read a big tags file.  You should use</div><div class='line' id='LC1171'>		more convenient include completion now.</div><div class='line' id='LC1172'><br/></div><div class='line' id='LC1173'>syntax_complete.vim				*syntax_complete*</div><div class='line' id='LC1174'>		This source analyzes a syntax file like</div><div class='line' id='LC1175'>		autoload/syntaxcomplete.vim offered by default, and to</div><div class='line' id='LC1176'>		add to candidate completion.  The plugin can recognize</div><div class='line' id='LC1177'>		candidates a lot more than autoload/syntaxcomplete.vim.</div><div class='line' id='LC1178'><br/></div><div class='line' id='LC1179'>include_complete.vim				*include_complete*</div><div class='line' id='LC1180'>		This source will add the file which an opening buffer</div><div class='line' id='LC1181'>		refers to to candidate.  It is convenient, because you do</div><div class='line' id='LC1182'>		not need to prepare a tags file and a dictionary file.</div><div class='line' id='LC1183'>		But it is necessary for &#39;path&#39; and &#39;include&#39;,</div><div class='line' id='LC1184'>		&#39;includeexpr&#39; to be set adequately.</div><div class='line' id='LC1185'><br/></div><div class='line' id='LC1186'>		Note: If you have vimproc installed, neocomplcache will cache</div><div class='line' id='LC1187'>		automatically.  Otherwise it won&#39;t; please execute</div><div class='line' id='LC1188'>		|:NeoComplCacheCachingInclude| manually.</div><div class='line' id='LC1189'><br/></div><div class='line' id='LC1190'>vim_complete.vim				*vim_complete*</div><div class='line' id='LC1191'>		This source analyzes context and start Omni completion of</div><div class='line' id='LC1192'>		Vim script.  This plugin does not work other than editing</div><div class='line' id='LC1193'>		time of Vim script.  I created it because neocomplcache</div><div class='line' id='LC1194'>		cannot call |i_CTRL-X_CTRL-V|.  Local variable and a</div><div class='line' id='LC1195'>		script variable, a function and the analysis of the</div><div class='line' id='LC1196'>		command are implemented now.</div><div class='line' id='LC1197'><br/></div><div class='line' id='LC1198'>dictionary_complete.vim				*dictionary_complete*</div><div class='line' id='LC1199'>		This source adds candidates from &#39;dictionary&#39; or</div><div class='line' id='LC1200'>		|g:neocomplcache_dictionary_filetype_lists|.</div><div class='line' id='LC1201'><br/></div><div class='line' id='LC1202'>filename_complete.vim				*filename_complete*</div><div class='line' id='LC1203'>		This source collects filename candidates.</div><div class='line' id='LC1204'><br/></div><div class='line' id='LC1205'>filename_include.vim				*filename_include*</div><div class='line' id='LC1206'>		This source collects filename candidates.  It is useful</div><div class='line' id='LC1207'>		when you input header file name.  It recognizes include</div><div class='line' id='LC1208'>		pattern and include path like include_complete.</div><div class='line' id='LC1209'><br/></div><div class='line' id='LC1210'>omni_complete.vim				*omni_complete*</div><div class='line' id='LC1211'>		This source calls &#39;omnifunc&#39; automatically when cursor</div><div class='line' id='LC1212'>		text is matched with |g:neocomplcache_omni_patterns|.  If</div><div class='line' id='LC1213'>		|g:neocomplcache_omni_function_list|is defined,</div><div class='line' id='LC1214'>		neocomplcache will give priority it.</div><div class='line' id='LC1215'>		Note: This source is not supported wildcard.</div><div class='line' id='LC1216'><br/></div><div class='line' id='LC1217'><br/></div><div class='line' id='LC1218'>suffix of complete candidates in popup menu declaration.</div><div class='line' id='LC1219'>(This will be good for user to know where candidate from and what it is.)</div><div class='line' id='LC1220'><br/></div><div class='line' id='LC1221'>&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;filename_complete          -&gt; [F] {filename}</div><div class='line' id='LC1222'>&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;filename_include           -&gt; [FI] {filename}</div><div class='line' id='LC1223'>&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;dictionary_complete        -&gt; [D] {words}</div><div class='line' id='LC1224'>&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;member_complete            -&gt; [M] member</div><div class='line' id='LC1225'>&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;buffer_complete            -&gt; [B] {buffername}</div><div class='line' id='LC1226'>&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;syntax_complete            -&gt; [S] {syntax-keyword}</div><div class='line' id='LC1227'>&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;include_complete           -&gt; [I]</div><div class='line' id='LC1228'>&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;neosnippet                 -&gt; [neosnip]</div><div class='line' id='LC1229'>&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;vim_complete               -&gt; [vim] type</div><div class='line' id='LC1230'>&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;omni_complete              -&gt; [O]</div><div class='line' id='LC1231'>&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;tags_complete              -&gt; [T]</div><div class='line' id='LC1232'>&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;other plugin sources       -&gt; [plugin-name-prefix]</div><div class='line' id='LC1233'>&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;other completefunc sources -&gt; [plugin-name-prefix]</div><div class='line' id='LC1234'>&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;other ftplugin sources     -&gt; [plugin-name-prefix]</div><div class='line' id='LC1235'><br/></div><div class='line' id='LC1236'>------------------------------------------------------------------------------</div><div class='line' id='LC1237'>USER SOURCES 					*neocomplcache-user-sources*</div><div class='line' id='LC1238'><br/></div><div class='line' id='LC1239'>This section, introduce non default neocomplcache sources.</div><div class='line' id='LC1240'><br/></div><div class='line' id='LC1241'>neosnippet				*neocomplcache-sources-neosnippet*</div><div class='line' id='LC1242'>		This source is for snippets completion.</div><div class='line' id='LC1243'>		Note: This source is not in default sources after</div><div class='line' id='LC1244'>		neocomplcache ver.7.0.</div><div class='line' id='LC1245'>		https://github.com/Shougo/neosnippet</div><div class='line' id='LC1246'><br/></div><div class='line' id='LC1247'>neco-ghc				*neocomplcache-sources-neco-ghc*</div><div class='line' id='LC1248'>		https://github.com/ujihisa/neco-ghc</div><div class='line' id='LC1249'>		eagletmt originally implemented and now ujihisa is maintaining</div><div class='line' id='LC1250'>		this source.  It completes a source file written in Haskell.</div><div class='line' id='LC1251'>		It requires ghc-mod &lt;http://www.mew.org/~kazu/proj/ghc-mod/&gt;.</div><div class='line' id='LC1252'><br/></div><div class='line' id='LC1253'>==============================================================================</div><div class='line' id='LC1254'>FILTERS						*neocomplcache-filters*</div><div class='line' id='LC1255'><br/></div><div class='line' id='LC1256'>To custom candidates, neocomplcache uses the filters. There are three kinds of</div><div class='line' id='LC1257'>filters are available. &quot;matcher&quot; is to use filter candidates. &quot;sorter&quot; is to</div><div class='line' id='LC1258'>use sort candidates. &quot;converter&quot; is to use candidates conversion.</div><div class='line' id='LC1259'><br/></div><div class='line' id='LC1260'>Note: &quot;matcher&quot; is not implemented. It will implemented in ver.8.1.</div><div class='line' id='LC1261'><br/></div><div class='line' id='LC1262'>Default sources are below. But you can create original filters(cf:</div><div class='line' id='LC1263'>|neocomplcache-create-filter|) and set them by</div><div class='line' id='LC1264'>|neocomplcache#custom_source()|.</div><div class='line' id='LC1265'>&gt;</div><div class='line' id='LC1266'>	call unite#custom_source(&#39;buffer_complete&#39;, &#39;converters&#39;, [])</div><div class='line' id='LC1267'><br/></div><div class='line' id='LC1268'>	&quot; Change default sorter.</div><div class='line' id='LC1269'>	call unite#custom_source(&#39;_&#39;, &#39;sorters&#39;,</div><div class='line' id='LC1270'>	\ [&#39;sorter_length&#39;])</div><div class='line' id='LC1271'>&lt;</div><div class='line' id='LC1272'>					*neocomplcache-filter-sorter_default*</div><div class='line' id='LC1273'>Default sorters: [&#39;sorter_rank&#39;].</div><div class='line' id='LC1274'><br/></div><div class='line' id='LC1275'>					*neocomplcache-filter-converter_default*</div><div class='line' id='LC1276'>Default converters: [&#39;converter_remove_next_keyword&#39;,</div><div class='line' id='LC1277'>&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;\      &#39;converter_delimiter&#39;, &#39;converter_case&#39;, &#39;converter_abbr&#39;].</div><div class='line' id='LC1278'><br/></div><div class='line' id='LC1279'>					*neocomplcache-filter-sorter_nothing*</div><div class='line' id='LC1280'>sorter_nothing	Nothing sorter.</div><div class='line' id='LC1281'><br/></div><div class='line' id='LC1282'>					*neocomplcache-filter-sorter_rank*</div><div class='line' id='LC1283'>sorter_rank	Matched rank order sorter.  The higher the matched word is</div><div class='line' id='LC1284'>		already selected or in current buffer</div><div class='line' id='LC1285'><br/></div><div class='line' id='LC1286'>					*neocomplcache-filter-sorter_length*</div><div class='line' id='LC1287'>sorter_length	Candidates length order sorter.</div><div class='line' id='LC1288'><br/></div><div class='line' id='LC1289'>					*neocomplcache-filter-converter_nothing*</div><div class='line' id='LC1290'>converter_nothing</div><div class='line' id='LC1291'>		This converter is dummy.</div><div class='line' id='LC1292'><br/></div><div class='line' id='LC1293'>					*neocomplcache-filter-converter_abbr*</div><div class='line' id='LC1294'>converter_abbr</div><div class='line' id='LC1295'>		The converter which abbreviates a candidate&#39;s abbr.</div><div class='line' id='LC1296'><br/></div><div class='line' id='LC1297'>					*neocomplcache-filter-converter_case*</div><div class='line' id='LC1298'>converter_case</div><div class='line' id='LC1299'>		The converter which converts a candidate&#39;s word in text mode.</div><div class='line' id='LC1300'>		(cf: |g:neocomplcache_text_mode_filetypes|)</div><div class='line' id='LC1301'><br/></div><div class='line' id='LC1302'>				*neocomplcache-filter-converter_delimiter*</div><div class='line' id='LC1303'>converter_delimiter</div><div class='line' id='LC1304'>		The converter which abbreviates a candidate&#39;s delimiter.</div><div class='line' id='LC1305'>		(cf: |g:neocomplcache_delimiter_patterns|)</div><div class='line' id='LC1306'><br/></div><div class='line' id='LC1307'>			*neocomplcache-filter-converter_remove_next_keyword*</div><div class='line' id='LC1308'>converter_remove_next_keyword</div><div class='line' id='LC1309'>		The converter which removes matched next keyword part in a</div><div class='line' id='LC1310'>		candidate&#39;s word.</div><div class='line' id='LC1311'>		(cf: |g:neocomplcache_next_keyword_patterns|)</div><div class='line' id='LC1312'><br/></div><div class='line' id='LC1313'>==============================================================================</div><div class='line' id='LC1314'>CREATE SOURCE					*neocomplcache-create-source*</div><div class='line' id='LC1315'><br/></div><div class='line' id='LC1316'>In this clause, I comment on a method to make source of neocomplcache.  The</div><div class='line' id='LC1317'>ability of neocomplcache will spread by creating source by yourself.</div><div class='line' id='LC1318'><br/></div><div class='line' id='LC1319'>The files in autoload/neocomplcache/sources are automatically loaded and it</div><div class='line' id='LC1320'>calls neocomplcache#sources#{source_name}#define() whose return value is the</div><div class='line' id='LC1321'>source.  Each return value can be a list so you can return an empty list to</div><div class='line' id='LC1322'>avoid adding undesirable sources.  To add your own sources dynamically, you</div><div class='line' id='LC1323'>can use |neocomplcache#define_source()|.</div><div class='line' id='LC1324'><br/></div><div class='line' id='LC1325'>------------------------------------------------------------------------------</div><div class='line' id='LC1326'>SOURCE ATTRIBUTES			*neocomplcache-source-attributes*</div><div class='line' id='LC1327'><br/></div><div class='line' id='LC1328'>					*neocomplcache-source-attribute-name*</div><div class='line' id='LC1329'>name			String		(Required)</div><div class='line' id='LC1330'>			The name of a source.  It must consist of the</div><div class='line' id='LC1331'>			following characters:</div><div class='line' id='LC1332'>			- a-z</div><div class='line' id='LC1333'>			- 0-9</div><div class='line' id='LC1334'>			- _</div><div class='line' id='LC1335'>			- /</div><div class='line' id='LC1336'>			- - (Not head)</div><div class='line' id='LC1337'><br/></div><div class='line' id='LC1338'>					*neocomplcache-source-attribute-kind*</div><div class='line' id='LC1339'>kind			String			(Optional)</div><div class='line' id='LC1340'>			Source kind.</div><div class='line' id='LC1341'>			Following values are available.</div><div class='line' id='LC1342'>			&quot;manual&quot;  : This source decides complete position</div><div class='line' id='LC1343'>			            manually.</div><div class='line' id='LC1344'>			            Note: &quot;complfunc&quot; or &quot;ftplugin&quot; are old</div><div class='line' id='LC1345'>				    values.</div><div class='line' id='LC1346'>			&quot;keyword&quot; : This source decides complete position by</div><div class='line' id='LC1347'>			           |g:neocomplcache_keyword_patterns|.</div><div class='line' id='LC1348'>			            Note: &quot;plugin&quot; is old value.</div><div class='line' id='LC1349'><br/></div><div class='line' id='LC1350'>				*neocomplcache-source-attribute-filetypes*</div><div class='line' id='LC1351'>filetypes		Dictionary		(Optional)</div><div class='line' id='LC1352'>			Available filetype dictionary.</div><div class='line' id='LC1353'><br/></div><div class='line' id='LC1354'>			For example:</div><div class='line' id='LC1355'>&gt;</div><div class='line' id='LC1356'>			let source = {</div><div class='line' id='LC1357'>			      \ &#39;name&#39; : &#39;test&#39;,</div><div class='line' id='LC1358'>			      \ &#39;kind&#39; : &#39;manual&#39;,</div><div class='line' id='LC1359'>			      \ &#39;filetypes&#39; : { &#39;vim&#39; : 1, &#39;html&#39; : 1 },</div><div class='line' id='LC1360'>			      \}</div><div class='line' id='LC1361'>&lt;</div><div class='line' id='LC1362'>			The source is available in vim and html filetypes.</div><div class='line' id='LC1363'><br/></div><div class='line' id='LC1364'>			If you omit it, this source available in all</div><div class='line' id='LC1365'>			filetypes.</div><div class='line' id='LC1366'><br/></div><div class='line' id='LC1367'><br/></div><div class='line' id='LC1368'>					*neocomplcache-source-attribute-rank*</div><div class='line' id='LC1369'>rank			Number		(Optional)</div><div class='line' id='LC1370'>			Source priority.</div><div class='line' id='LC1371'>			Note: You can set source priority by</div><div class='line' id='LC1372'>			|g:neocomplcache_source_rank|, but it is obsolete way.</div><div class='line' id='LC1373'><br/></div><div class='line' id='LC1374'>			If you omit it, it is set below value.</div><div class='line' id='LC1375'>			If kind attribute is &quot;keyword&quot; : 5</div><div class='line' id='LC1376'>			If filetype attribute is empty : 10</div><div class='line' id='LC1377'>			Else : 100</div><div class='line' id='LC1378'><br/></div><div class='line' id='LC1379'>			*neocomplcache-source-attribute-min_pattern_length*</div><div class='line' id='LC1380'>min_pattern_length</div><div class='line' id='LC1381'>			Number		(Optional)</div><div class='line' id='LC1382'>			Required pattern length for completion.</div><div class='line' id='LC1383'><br/></div><div class='line' id='LC1384'>			If you omit it, it is set below value.</div><div class='line' id='LC1385'>			If kind attribute is &quot;keyword&quot; :</div><div class='line' id='LC1386'>			    |g:neocomplcache_auto_completion_start_length|</div><div class='line' id='LC1387'>			Else : 0</div><div class='line' id='LC1388'><br/></div><div class='line' id='LC1389'>			*neocomplcache-source-attribute-max_candidates*</div><div class='line' id='LC1390'>max_candidates</div><div class='line' id='LC1391'>			Number		(Optional)</div><div class='line' id='LC1392'>			The maximum number of candidates.</div><div class='line' id='LC1393'><br/></div><div class='line' id='LC1394'>			This attribute is optional; if it is not given,</div><div class='line' id='LC1395'>			0 is used as the default value.  This means</div><div class='line' id='LC1396'>			maximum number is infinity.</div><div class='line' id='LC1397'><br/></div><div class='line' id='LC1398'>					*neocomplcache-source-attribute-hooks*</div><div class='line' id='LC1399'>hooks			Dictionary		(Optional)</div><div class='line' id='LC1400'>			You may put hook functions in this dictionary in which</div><div class='line' id='LC1401'>			the key is the position to hook and the value is the</div><div class='line' id='LC1402'>			reference to the function to be called.  The following</div><div class='line' id='LC1403'>			hook functions are defined:</div><div class='line' id='LC1404'><br/></div><div class='line' id='LC1405'>				*neocomplcache-source-attribute-hooks-on_init*</div><div class='line' id='LC1406'>			on_init</div><div class='line' id='LC1407'>			Called when initializing the source.</div><div class='line' id='LC1408'>			This function takes {context} as its parameters.</div><div class='line' id='LC1409'>				*neocomplcache-source-attribute-initialize*</div><div class='line' id='LC1410'>			Note initialize() attribute is obsolete interface for</div><div class='line' id='LC1411'>			initialization.</div><div class='line' id='LC1412'><br/></div><div class='line' id='LC1413'>				*neocomplcache-source-attribute-hooks-on_final*</div><div class='line' id='LC1414'>			on_final</div><div class='line' id='LC1415'>			Called after executing |:NeoComplCacheDisable|.</div><div class='line' id='LC1416'>			This function takes {context} as its parameters.</div><div class='line' id='LC1417'>				*neocomplcache-source-attribute-finalize*</div><div class='line' id='LC1418'>			Note finalize() attribute is obsolete interface for</div><div class='line' id='LC1419'>			finalization.</div><div class='line' id='LC1420'><br/></div><div class='line' id='LC1421'>			*neocomplcache-source-attribute-hooks-on_post_filter*</div><div class='line' id='LC1422'>			on_post_filter</div><div class='line' id='LC1423'>			Called after the filters to narrow down the</div><div class='line' id='LC1424'>			candidates.  This is used to set attributes. This</div><div class='line' id='LC1425'>			filters is to avoid adversely affecting the</div><div class='line' id='LC1426'>			performance.</div><div class='line' id='LC1427'>			This function takes {context} as its parameters.</div><div class='line' id='LC1428'><br/></div><div class='line' id='LC1429'>			*neocomplcache-source-attribute-get_complete_position*</div><div class='line' id='LC1430'>get_complete_position	Function	(Optional)</div><div class='line' id='LC1431'>			This function takes {context} as its</div><div class='line' id='LC1432'>			parameter and returns complete position in current</div><div class='line' id='LC1433'>			line.</div><div class='line' id='LC1434'>			Here, {context} is the context information when the</div><div class='line' id='LC1435'>			source is called(|neocomplcache-notation-{context}|).</div><div class='line' id='LC1436'>			If you omit it, neocomplcache will use the position</div><div class='line' id='LC1437'>			using |g:neocomplcache_keyword_patterns|.</div><div class='line' id='LC1438'>			Note get_keyword_pos() is obsolete interface for</div><div class='line' id='LC1439'>			get complete position.</div><div class='line' id='LC1440'><br/></div><div class='line' id='LC1441'>			*neocomplcache-source-attribute-gather_candidates*</div><div class='line' id='LC1442'>gather_candidates	Function	(Required)</div><div class='line' id='LC1443'>			This function is called in gathering candidates.  If</div><div class='line' id='LC1444'>			you enabled fuzzy completion by</div><div class='line' id='LC1445'>			|g:neocomplcache_enable_fuzzy_completion| , this</div><div class='line' id='LC1446'>			function is called whenever the input string is</div><div class='line' id='LC1447'>			changed.  This function takes {context} as its</div><div class='line' id='LC1448'>			parameter and returns a list of {candidate}.</div><div class='line' id='LC1449'>			Here, {context} is the context information when the</div><div class='line' id='LC1450'>			source is called(|neocomplcache-notation-{context}|).</div><div class='line' id='LC1451'>			Note: get_complete_words() and get_keyword_list() are</div><div class='line' id='LC1452'>			obsolete interface for gather candidates.</div><div class='line' id='LC1453'>			Note: |neocomplcache-filters| feature is disabled for</div><div class='line' id='LC1454'>			compatibility in neocomplcache ver.8.0. You should use</div><div class='line' id='LC1455'>			new interface in neocomplcache ver.8.1.</div><div class='line' id='LC1456'><br/></div><div class='line' id='LC1457'>{context}				*neocomplcache-notation-{context}*</div><div class='line' id='LC1458'>			A dictionary to give context information.</div><div class='line' id='LC1459'>			The followings are the primary information.</div><div class='line' id='LC1460'>			The global context information can be acquired</div><div class='line' id='LC1461'>			by |neocomplcache#get_context()|.</div><div class='line' id='LC1462'><br/></div><div class='line' id='LC1463'>			input			(String)</div><div class='line' id='LC1464'>				The input string of current line.</div><div class='line' id='LC1465'><br/></div><div class='line' id='LC1466'>			complete_pos		(Number)</div><div class='line' id='LC1467'>				The complete position of current source.</div><div class='line' id='LC1468'><br/></div><div class='line' id='LC1469'>			complete_str		(String)</div><div class='line' id='LC1470'>				The complete string of current source.</div><div class='line' id='LC1471'><br/></div><div class='line' id='LC1472'>			source__{name}		(Unknown)	(Optional)</div><div class='line' id='LC1473'>				Additional source information.</div><div class='line' id='LC1474'>				Note: Recommend sources save</div><div class='line' id='LC1475'>				variables instead of s: variables.</div><div class='line' id='LC1476'><br/></div><div class='line' id='LC1477'>------------------------------------------------------------------------------</div><div class='line' id='LC1478'>CANDIDATE ATTRIBUTES			*neocomplcache-candidate-attributes*</div><div class='line' id='LC1479'><br/></div><div class='line' id='LC1480'>				*neocomplcache-candidate-attribute-name*</div><div class='line' id='LC1481'>word			String		(Required)</div><div class='line' id='LC1482'>			The completion word of a candidate. It is used for</div><div class='line' id='LC1483'>			matching inputs.</div><div class='line' id='LC1484'><br/></div><div class='line' id='LC1485'>				*neocomplcache-candidate-attribute-abbr*</div><div class='line' id='LC1486'>abbr			String		(Optional)</div><div class='line' id='LC1487'>			The abbreviation of a candidate. It is displayed in</div><div class='line' id='LC1488'>			popup window. It is omitted by</div><div class='line' id='LC1489'>			|g:neocomplcache_max_keyword_width|.</div><div class='line' id='LC1490'><br/></div><div class='line' id='LC1491'>				*neocomplcache-candidate-attribute-kind*</div><div class='line' id='LC1492'>kind			String		(Optional)</div><div class='line' id='LC1493'>			The kind of a candidate. It is displayed in popup</div><div class='line' id='LC1494'>			window.</div><div class='line' id='LC1495'><br/></div><div class='line' id='LC1496'>				*neocomplcache-candidate-attribute-menu*</div><div class='line' id='LC1497'>menu			String		(Optional)</div><div class='line' id='LC1498'>			The menu information of a candidate. It is displayed</div><div class='line' id='LC1499'>			in popup window.</div><div class='line' id='LC1500'><br/></div><div class='line' id='LC1501'>				*neocomplcache-candidate-attribute-info*</div><div class='line' id='LC1502'>info			String		(Optional)</div><div class='line' id='LC1503'>			The preview information of a candidate. If</div><div class='line' id='LC1504'>			&#39;completeopt&#39; contains &quot;preview&quot;, it will be displayed</div><div class='line' id='LC1505'>			in |preview-window|.</div><div class='line' id='LC1506'><br/></div><div class='line' id='LC1507'>				*neocomplcache-candidate-attribute-rank*</div><div class='line' id='LC1508'>rank			Number		(Optional)</div><div class='line' id='LC1509'>			The completion priority.</div><div class='line' id='LC1510'><br/></div><div class='line' id='LC1511'><br/></div><div class='line' id='LC1512'>CONTEXT						*neocomplcache-context*</div><div class='line' id='LC1513'><br/></div><div class='line' id='LC1514'>==============================================================================</div><div class='line' id='LC1515'>CREATE FILTER					*neocomplcache-create-filter*</div><div class='line' id='LC1516'><br/></div><div class='line' id='LC1517'>The files in autoload/neocomplcache/filters are automatically loaded and it</div><div class='line' id='LC1518'>calls neocomplcache#filters#{filter_name}#define() whose return value is the</div><div class='line' id='LC1519'>filter.  Each return value can be a list so you can return an empty list to</div><div class='line' id='LC1520'>avoid adding undesirable filters.  To add your own filters dynamically, you</div><div class='line' id='LC1521'>can use |neocomplcache#define_filter()|.</div><div class='line' id='LC1522'><br/></div><div class='line' id='LC1523'>------------------------------------------------------------------------------</div><div class='line' id='LC1524'>FILTER ATTRIBUTES			*neocomplcache-filter-attributes*</div><div class='line' id='LC1525'><br/></div><div class='line' id='LC1526'><br/></div><div class='line' id='LC1527'>					*neocomplcache-filter-attribute-name*</div><div class='line' id='LC1528'>name			String		(Required)</div><div class='line' id='LC1529'>			The filter name.</div><div class='line' id='LC1530'><br/></div><div class='line' id='LC1531'>					*neocomplcache-filter-attribute-filter*</div><div class='line' id='LC1532'>filter			Function		(Required)</div><div class='line' id='LC1533'>			The filter function.  This function takes {context} as</div><div class='line' id='LC1534'>			its parameter and returns a list of {candidate}.</div><div class='line' id='LC1535'>			The specification of the parameters and the returned</div><div class='line' id='LC1536'>			value is same as</div><div class='line' id='LC1537'>			|neocomplcache-source-attribute-gather_candidates|.</div><div class='line' id='LC1538'><br/></div><div class='line' id='LC1539'>					*neocomplcache-filter-attribute-description*</div><div class='line' id='LC1540'>description		String		(Optional)</div><div class='line' id='LC1541'>			The filter description string.</div><div class='line' id='LC1542'><br/></div><div class='line' id='LC1543'>==============================================================================</div><div class='line' id='LC1544'>UNITE SOURCES					*neocomplcache-unite-sources*</div><div class='line' id='LC1545'><br/></div><div class='line' id='LC1546'>				*neocomplcache-unite-source-neocomplcache*</div><div class='line' id='LC1547'>neocomplcache</div><div class='line' id='LC1548'>		Nominates neocomplcache completion candidates.  The kind is</div><div class='line' id='LC1549'>		&quot;completion&quot;.  This source is used in</div><div class='line' id='LC1550'>		|&lt;Plug&gt;(neocomplcache_start_unite_complete)|.</div><div class='line' id='LC1551'>&gt;</div><div class='line' id='LC1552'>		imap &lt;C-k&gt;  &lt;Plug&gt;(neocomplcache_start_unite_complete)</div><div class='line' id='LC1553'>		imap &lt;C-q&gt;  &lt;Plug&gt;(neocomplcache_start_unite_quick_match)</div><div class='line' id='LC1554'>&lt;</div><div class='line' id='LC1555'>==============================================================================</div><div class='line' id='LC1556'>FAQ						*neocomplcache-faq*</div><div class='line' id='LC1557'><br/></div><div class='line' id='LC1558'>Q: My customization for neocomplcache is invalid. Why?</div><div class='line' id='LC1559'><br/></div><div class='line' id='LC1560'>A: User customization for neocomplcache must be set before initialization of</div><div class='line' id='LC1561'>neocomplcache. For example: |neocomplcache#custom_source()|</div><div class='line' id='LC1562'><br/></div><div class='line' id='LC1563'>Q: Is there a way to control the colors used for popup menu using highlight</div><div class='line' id='LC1564'>groups?:</div><div class='line' id='LC1565'><br/></div><div class='line' id='LC1566'>A: Like this:</div><div class='line' id='LC1567'>&gt;</div><div class='line' id='LC1568'>	highlight Pmenu ctermbg=8 guibg=#606060</div><div class='line' id='LC1569'>	highlight PmenuSel ctermbg=1 guifg=#dddd00 guibg=#1f82cd</div><div class='line' id='LC1570'>	highlight PmenuSbar ctermbg=0 guibg=#d6d6d6</div><div class='line' id='LC1571'>&lt;</div><div class='line' id='LC1572'><br/></div><div class='line' id='LC1573'>Q: Python (or Ruby) interface crashes Vim when I use neocomplcache or not</div><div class='line' id='LC1574'>responding when input &quot;.&quot;:</div><div class='line' id='LC1575'><br/></div><div class='line' id='LC1576'>A: This is not neocomplcache&#39;s issue.  Please report to the maintainers of the</div><div class='line' id='LC1577'>omnicomplete (rubycomplete or pythoncomplete) and its Vim interface. Python interface is not available on every Vim environment. For example,</div><div class='line' id='LC1817'>&nbsp;Android, iOS, non configured Vim, or etc.</div><div class='line' id='LC1818'>&nbsp;2. Incompatibility between Python2 and Python3. I must rewrite for it.</div><div class='line' id='LC1819'>&nbsp;3. Loading Python interface is slow (10~20ms), but loading Lua interface is</div><div class='line' id='LC1820'>&nbsp;absolutely fast (270ns).</div><div class='line' id='LC1821'>&nbsp;4. Python2 and Python3 are not loaded at the same time on Unix environment.</div><div class='line' id='LC1822'>&nbsp;5. Python itself is too large.</div><div class='line' id='LC1823'>&nbsp;6. Python interface is slower than Lua interface (almost twice.)</div><div class='line' id='LC1824'>&nbsp;7. Lua interface is stable (no crashes on latest Vim.)</div><div class='line' id='LC1825'>&nbsp;8. Using C module (like vimproc, YouCompleteMe) is hard to compile on Windows</div><div class='line' id='LC1826'>&nbsp;environment.</div><div class='line' id='LC1827'>&nbsp;9. Using both Python and C, like YouCompleteMe, is too unstable. Your Vim may</div><div class='line' id='LC1828'>&nbsp;crashes or causes mysterious errors.</div><div class='line' id='LC1829'>&nbsp;10. To build if_lua is easy.</div><div class='line' id='LC1830'>&nbsp;11. I think if_lua is the second level language in Vim (The first is Vim</div><div class='line' id='LC1831'>&nbsp;script.)</div><div class='line' id='LC1832'><br/></div><div class='line' id='LC1833'>Q: I want to disable preview window.</div><div class='line' id='LC1834'><br/></div><div class='line' id='LC1835'>A:</div><div class='line' id='LC1836'>&gt;</div><div class='line' id='LC1837'>	set completeopt-=preview</div><div class='line' id='LC1838'>&lt;</div><div class='line' id='LC1839'><br/></div><div class='line' id='LC1840'>Q: I want to use &quot;vim-lua-ftplugin&quot;.</div><div class='line' id='LC1841'>https://github.com/xolox/vim-lua-ftplugin</div><div class='line' id='LC1842'><br/></div><div class='line' id='LC1843'>A: Please set |g:neocomplcache_omni_patterns| as below.</div><div class='line' id='LC1844'>Note: You can not use &quot;vim-lua-ftplugin&quot; Because &quot;longest&quot; completeopt conflicts with auto</div><div class='line' id='LC1882'>completion.  To use &quot;longest&quot; option, you must disable auto completion.</div><div class='line' id='LC1883'>&quot;longest&quot; is good feature. But it is for manual completion only.</div><div class='line' id='LC1884'><br/></div><div class='line' id='LC1885'>Q: autoclose conflicts with neocomplcache.</div><div class='line' id='LC1886'>https://github.com/Shougo/neocomplcache.vim/issues/350</div><div class='line' id='LC1887'><br/></div><div class='line' id='LC1888'>A: It is autoclose mappings problem. I cannot fix it. You should use</div><div class='line' id='LC1889'>auto-pairs plugin instead of it.</div><div class='line' id='LC1890'>https://github.com/jiangmiao/auto-pairs</div><div class='line' id='LC1891'><br/></div><div class='line' id='LC1892'>==============================================================================</div><div class='line' id='LC1893'>vim:tw=78:ts=8:ft=help:norl:noet:fen:noet:</div></pre></div></td>
          </tr>
        </table>
  </div>
